Case 110-Title: Tea Fruitcake
Ingredients: ["1 cup golden raisins", "1 cup dried currants", "3/4 cup dried cherries", "3/4 cup dried apricots, chopped", "1 1/2 cups walnuts, chopped", "Zest of 1 lemon", "3/4 cup brandy", "2 sticks butter", "1 cup packed brown sugar", "2 eggs", "2 cups all-purpose flour", "1/2 teaspoon salt", "1 tablespoon baking powder", "1 teaspoon ground cinnamon", "1/2 teaspoon allspice", "1/4 teaspoon freshly ground nutmeg", "3/4 cup orange juice", "1/2 cup brandy"]
Directions: ["In a medium sized bowl mix together the raisins, currants, cherries, apricots, walnuts, lemon zest and brandy.", "Cover and allow to macerate, covered in the refrigerator for at least 24 hours and up to 7 days, stirring occasionally.", "Drain off any excess liquid before making batter.", "Preheat oven to 350 degrees F. Butter and flour two 9 by 5-inch loaf pans.", "In an electric mixer cream the butter and the brown sugar until light and fluffy.", "Add the eggs one at a time and beat well.", "Sift together the dry ingredients and toss 1/2-cup of this mixture with the fruits.", "Add the remainder of the dry ingredients in 2 batches to the butter mixture, alternating with the orange juice and brandy.", "Beat until incorporated.", "Fold in the floured fruits and spoon batter equally into the prepared pans.", "Bake for 1 hour 15 minutes to 1 hour and a half or until a toothpick inserted comes out clean."]
Requirement: Sulfite-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Modified Tea Fruitcake Recipe**

Ingredients:
- 1 cup organic golden raisins (ensure no sulfites added)
- 1 cup organic dried currants (ensure no sulfites added)
- 3/4 cup organic dried cherries (ensure no sulfites added)
- 3/4 cup organic dried apricots, chopped (ensure no sulfites added)
- 1 1/2 cups walnuts, chopped
- Zest of 1 lemon
- 3/4 cup apple juice
- 2 sticks unsalted butter
- 1 cup packed organic brown sugar (ensure no sulfites added)
- 2 eggs
- 2 cups all-purpose flour
- 1/2 teaspoon salt
- 1 tablespoon baking powder
- 1 teaspoon ground cinnamon
- 1/2 teaspoon allspice
- 1/4 teaspoon freshly ground nutmeg
- 3/4 cup freshly squeezed orange juice
- 1/2 cup apple juice

Instructions:
1. In a medium-sized bowl, mix together the raisins, currants, cherries, apricots, walnuts, lemon zest, and 3/4 cup apple juice.
2. Cover and allow to macerate in the refrigerator for at least 24 hours and up to 7 days, stirring occasionally.
3. Drain off any excess liquid before making the batter.
4. Preheat the oven to 350 degrees F. Butter and flour two 9 by 5-inch loaf pans.
5. In an electric mixer, cream the butter and the brown sugar until light and fluffy.
6. Add the eggs one at a time and beat well.
7. Sift together the dry ingredients and toss 1/2-cup of this mixture with the fruits.
8. Add the remainder of the dry ingredients in 2 batches to the butter mixture, alternating with the orange juice and 1/2 cup apple juice.
9. Beat until incorporated.
10. Fold in the floured fruits and spoon batter equally into the prepared pans.
11. Bake for 1 hour 15 minutes to 1 hour and a half or until a toothpick inserted comes out clean.
```

```markdown
**Modified Recipe: Peanut-free Noodle Casserole**

- 8 oz. fine noodles, cooked
- 1 cup plain Greek yogurt (as a substitute for sour cream)
- 1 cup fine (small curd) cottage cheese
- Salt to taste
- 1 onion, finely chopped
- 1 Tbsp. Worcestershire sauce (ensure peanut-free variety)
- Grated Parmesan cheese

**Instructions:**
```

Case 112-Title: Ceviche Tostadas
Ingredients: ["8 5 1/2-inch extra-thin corn tortillas, or prepared tostada shells", "Vegetable oil for frying", "1 pound orange roughy, red snapper or other fish fillet", "1 1/4 cups Key lime juice, or 1 cup lime juice and 1/4 cup lemon juice", "1 tablespoon salt", "1/2 teaspoon dried oregano", "2 heaping tablespoons cilantro, coarsely chopped", "1/4 red onion, thinly sliced", "1 medium tomato, diced", "Freshly ground black pepper to taste", "Hot sauce (optional)"]
Directions: ["To make tostada shells, lay tortillas in a single layer on a counter and cover with a dry towel for about 30 minutes.", "Heat oil to 1-inch depth in a large skillet to 380 degrees.", "Fry one at a time until golden, about 30 seconds per side.", "Drain on paper towels.", "Cut fish into half-inch dice.", "Marinate in lime juice and salt to cover for 1 to 6 hours.", "Drain fish, mix with remaining ingredients and serve on the crisped tortillas with lime wedges, or use as a dip with tortilla chips."]
Requirement: Soy-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
### Modified Ceviche Tostadas Recipe (Soy-Free)

#### Ingredients
- 8 5 1/2-inch extra-thin corn tortillas, or prepared tostada shells
- High-oleic safflower oil or avocado oil for frying
- 1 pound orange roughy, red snapper, or other fish fillet
- 1 1/4 cups Key lime juice, or 1 cup lime juice and 1/4 cup lemon juice
- 1 tablespoon salt
- 1/2 teaspoon dried oregano
- 2 heaping tablespoons cilantro, coarsely chopped
- 1/4 red onion, thinly sliced
- 1 medium tomato, diced
- Freshly ground black pepper to taste
- Hot sauce (optional, ensure soy-free label)

#### Instructions
1. **Prepare Tostada Shells:**
   - Lay tortillas in a single layer on a counter and cover with a dry towel for about 30 minutes to slightly dry out.

2. **Frying Tostadas:**
   - Heat safflower or avocado oil to 1-inch depth in a large skillet to 380 degrees Fahrenheit.
   - Fry one tortilla at a time until golden, about 30 seconds per side.
   - Drain fried tortillas on paper towels.

3. **Prepare Ceviche:**
   - Cut fish into half-inch dice.
   - Marinate fish in lime juice and salt, ensuring the fish is completely covered, for 1 to 6 hours in the refrigerator.

4. **Assemble:**
   - Drain the marinated fish.
   - Mix drained fish with dried oregano, cilantro, red onion, diced tomato, and freshly ground black pepper.
   - Serve the fish mixture on crisped tortillas.
   - Optionally, serve with lime wedges and soy-free hot sauce if desired.
```

Case 113-Title: Boston Marlborough Pie Recipe
Ingredients: ["1 cup tart applesauce, sieved", "3 tablespoons lemon juice", "1 cup sugar", "4 eggs, slightly beaten", "2 tablespoons butter, melted", "1/2 teaspoon nutmeg (optional)", "1/2 teaspoon salt", "One 9-inch unbaked pastry shell (deep)"]
Directions: ["Preheat oven to 450\u00b0F. Whisk together applesauce, lemon juice, sugar, eggs, butter, nutmeg, and salt. Pour into pastry shell. Bake at 450\u00b0 for 15 minutes, reduce heat to 275\u00b0 and bake until pie is fully set, about 1 hour longer."]
Requirement: Gluten-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
### Boston Marlborough Pie (Gluten-Free)

#### Ingredients:
- 1 cup tart applesauce, sieved
- 3 tablespoons lemon juice
- 1 cup sugar
- 4 eggs, slightly beaten
- 2 tablespoons unsalted butter, melted (ensure gluten-free, check label)
- 1/2 teaspoon nutmeg (optional)
- 1/2 teaspoon salt
- One 9-inch gluten-free pastry shell (deep)

#### Directions:
1. Preheat oven to 450°F (232°C).
2. In a large mixing bowl, whisk together the applesauce, lemon juice, sugar, eggs, melted butter, nutmeg, and salt until smoothly combined.
3. Pour the mixture into the prepared gluten-free pastry shell, ensuring an even distribution.
4. Place the pie in the preheated oven and bake for 15 minutes at 450°F (232°C).
5. After 15 minutes, reduce the oven temperature to 275°F (135°C) and continue baking until the pie is fully set, approximately 1 hour longer.
6. Remove from oven and allow to cool before serving. Enjoy your gluten-free Boston Marlborough Pie!
```

```markdown
**Modified Creamed Rice Recipe**

**Ingredients:**
- 2 cups cooked rice
- 1 cup shredded corn-free cheese (such as cheddar or a salt-brined cheese, ensuring it is corn-free)
- 1/2 cup butter (ensure corn-free or use ghee)
- 3/4 cup chopped celery
- 3/4 cup chopped onion
- 2 packages frozen chopped broccoli (verify corn-free label)
- 1 can homemade corn-free cream of mushroom soup (recipe below)

**Corn-Free Cream of Mushroom Soup Ingredients:**
- 1 tablespoon butter (ensure corn-free)
- 1 cup finely chopped mushrooms
- 2 tablespoons gluten-free all-purpose flour (made with rice or potato flour, corn-free)
- 1 cup milk (or dairy-free milk of choice)
- 1/2 cup vegetable broth (ensure corn-free)
- Salt and pepper to taste

**Instructions for Corn-Free Cream of Mushroom Soup:**
1. In a saucepan, melt butter over medium heat. Add chopped mushrooms and cook until tender.
2. Sprinkle gluten-free flour over the mushrooms and stir for 1 minute.
3. Gradually whisk in milk and vegetable broth, stirring constantly until the mixture thickens.
4. Season with salt and pepper, then remove from heat and set aside.

**Instructions for Creamed Rice:**
1. Preheat oven to 350°F (175°C).
2. Combine hot cooked rice with shredded corn-free cheese in a large mixing bowl.
3. In a skillet, melt butter over medium heat. Add celery and onion, sauté until softened.
4. Boil broccoli in a large pot of water until tender. Drain well.
5. In the large mixing bowl with the rice and cheese, add the sautéed celery and onion, drained broccoli, and homemade cream of mushroom soup.
6. Stir all ingredients until well combined.
7. Transfer the mixture to a casserole dish.
8. Bake in preheated oven for 45 minutes to 1 hour, or until the top is golden brown and the mixture is bubbly.
9. Allow to cool slightly before serving.
```

Caution

   - Specify and ensure that the dairy and vegetable broth used in the homemade soup are verified corn-free.

2. **Cross-Contamination Risk:**
   - Ensure all kitchen utensils, pots, pans, and surfaces are thoroughly cleaned to prevent any corn contamination.
   - Verify that any pre-packaged or processed ingredients are handled in facilities that prevent cross-contamination with corn. 

3. **Home Preparation Caution:**
   - During the preparation of homemade corn-free cream of mushroom soup, ensure that all ingredients used, particularly flour and broth, are handled and prepared in a corn-free environment.

These points need careful consideration and verification to make the modified recipe fully compliant with the corn-free requirement.

```markdown
**Modified Sweet Potato Salad Recipe (Corn-Free)**

- 2 medium-sized sweet potatoes (about 1 lb.)
- 1 small green pepper, cut into 1-inch pieces
- 2 Tbsp. chopped green onions
- 1 Tbsp. chopped fresh parsley
- Green leaf lettuce (optional)

- 1 tsp. water
- 1 tsp. olive oil
- 1/8 tsp. salt
```

Case 117-Title: Baked Macaroni And Cheese
Ingredients: ["2 quarts water", "salt", "8 ounces elbow macaroni", "4 tablespoons butter or 4 tablespoons margarine", "1 1/2 cups seasoned dry bread crumbs", "1 small onion (minced)", "1 tablespoon flour", "1/4 teaspoon dry mustard", "1/8 teaspoon pepper", "1 1/2 cups milk", "1 1/2 cups Velveeta cheese (cubed into 1/4-inch chunks)", "1/2 cup shredded cheddar cheese"]
Directions: ["Boil water with 1 tsp salt in 3-qt saucepan.", "Add macaroni and cook until tender but firm.", "Drain.", "Grease 2-qt baking dish and preheat oven to 350\u00b0F.", "In 1-qt saucepan over medium heat, melt 2 tbsp butter and toss in breadcrumbs.", "Set aside.", "In 2-qt saucepan over medium heat, melt remaining butter.", "Add onion and cook until tender, about 5 minute.", "Blend in flour, mustard, pepper and 1 tsp salt.", "Stir in milk; cook until thickened - stirring continuously. Remove from heat, stir in cheese.", "Pour macaroni into baking dish and pour cheese over macaroni.", "Sprinkle crumb mixture over top.", "Bake for 20 minutes uncovered."]
Requirement: Corn-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Dish Name:** Corn-Free Baked Macaroni and Cheese

**Ingredients:**
- 2 quarts water
- 1 teaspoon salt (plus more for taste)
- 8 ounces corn-free elbow macaroni
- 4 tablespoons unsalted butter
- 1 1/2 cups corn-free dry bread crumbs
- 1 small onion (minced)
- 1 tablespoon all-purpose flour (ensured corn-free)
- 1/4 teaspoon dry mustard
- 1/8 teaspoon black pepper
- 1 1/2 cups whole milk (ensure no corn derivatives)
- 1 1/2 cups cream cheese (certified corn-free, cubed into 1/4-inch chunks)
- 1/2 cup shredded cheddar cheese (certified corn-free)

**Directions:**
1. Preheat the oven to 350°F (175°C) and grease a 2-quart baking dish.
2. In a 3-quart saucepan, bring water and 1 teaspoon of salt to a boil.
3. Add the macaroni and cook until tender but firm. Drain and set aside.
4. In a saucepan over medium heat, melt 2 tablespoons of butter, then mix in the corn-free breadcrumbs. Set aside.
5. In another saucepan, melt the remaining 2 tablespoons of butter over medium heat.
6. Add the minced onion and cook until tender, about 5 minutes.
7. Blend in the flour, dry mustard, pepper, and an additional teaspoon of salt.
8. Gradually stir in the milk and cook until the mixture thickens, stirring continuously.
9. Remove from heat and stir in the cream cheese and cheddar cheese until fully melted and smooth.
10. Combine the cooked macaroni and cheese sauce in the greased baking dish.
11. Sprinkle the buttered crumb mixture evenly over the top.
12. Bake uncovered in the preheated oven for 20 minutes or until the top is golden and crispy.

**Note:** Always verify that all packaged ingredients are certified corn-free to ensure against cross-contamination.
```

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

The modified recipe attempts to be corn-free by substituting and ensuring certified corn-free versions of ingredients such as elbow macaroni, bread crumbs, all-purpose flour, milk, cream cheese, and cheddar cheese. Here's what needs attention:

- Ensure that all substituted and mentioned ingredients are explicitly certified as corn-free, including avoiding corn derivatives in processing. This needs careful attention as cross-contamination and inadvertent inclusion of corn derivatives can occur in packaged foods.

- Although cream cheese and cheddar cheese are generally corn-free, it's important these are certified corn-free to exclude any additives or manufacturing processes involving corn.

Always double-check these certificates and consult with manufacturers if unsure to prevent potential risk for those with corn allergies or sensitivities.

Case 119-Title: Summer Time Turkey Club

Requirement: Peanut-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Dish Name:** Summer Time Turkey Club (Peanut-Free)

**Modified Recipe:**
Ingredients:
- 4 slices multigrain bread
- 6 slices honey roasted turkey meat
- 2 slices provolone cheese
- 1 medium tomato
- 1 small avocado
- 1 hard-boiled egg
- 2 tablespoons mayonnaise (ensure peanut-free)
- 2 teaspoons fresh basil leaves (approximately 12 leaves)
- Alfalfa sprouts
- Honey dijon mustard (ensure peanut-free)

**Instructions:**
1. Lightly toast the bread slices.
2. Slice the hard-boiled egg (lengthwise) into 4 slices.
3. Cut the tomato into 4 slices.
4. Thinly slice the avocado (lengthwise).
5. Place the mayonnaise in a small bowl.
6. Chop basil leaves and add to the mayonnaise, mixing well.
7. Begin making both sandwiches by spreading the basil-mayo mixture onto 2 slices of bread.
8. Top each slice with provolone cheese.
9. Lay sprouts over the cheese.
10. Place 2 tomato slices on top of the sprouts (2 tomato slices per bread slice).
11. Add 3 slices of turkey to each sandwich.
12. Add 2 slices of hard-boiled egg on top of the turkey.
13. Add the avocado slices.
14. Spread honey dijon mustard onto the remaining bread slices.
15. Add each slice on top of the prepared sandwiches.
16. Cut sandwiches in half and serve.
```

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

The modified recipe addresses the peanut-free requirement by specifying that both the mayonnaise and the honey dijon mustard should be ensured as peanut-free. However, to fully ensure safety for individuals with peanut allergies, the following points need to be watched out:

1. **Cross-Contamination Risk**: Verify that all the ingredients, including the bread, turkey meat, provolone cheese, and alfalfa sprouts, are sourced from facilities that are certified to be free from cross-contamination with peanuts. This information is not explicitly given in the modified recipe.

2. **Ingredient Certification**: Both the mayonnaise and honey dijon mustard need to be confirmed and potentially certified peanut-free. The recipe notes this, but it is essential that this is reliably checked and verified.

3. **Incomplete Labeling Details**: While the recipe insists on ensuring certain ingredients are “peanut-free,” additional vigilance is needed for all components, such as ensuring the bread does not contain peanut flour or is baked in facilities processing peanuts.

```markdown
**Modified Recipe: Ground Beef And Vegetables**

**Ingredients:**
- 1 lb ground beef
- 2 large potatoes, peeled and cut in chunks
- 1 onion, diced (or 2 cloves garlic, minced)
- 1/2 head cabbage, chopped
- 2 large carrots, peeled and sliced
- 1 cup green beans, trimmed and cut into pieces
- 1/2 cup tomato paste (ensure it is lupin-free)
- Salt, if desired
- Black pepper, to taste
- 1 tbsp olive oil

**Directions:**

5. Season with salt and black pepper to taste, if desired.
6. Cover the pan and cook on medium-low heat, stirring occasionally, for about 20 minutes or until the vegetables are tender.
7. Stir in the tomato paste, ensuring it's well distributed. Cover the pan again and cook for an additional 5 minutes.
8. Serve hot.
```

Case 123-Title: Buttermilk Blue Potatoes Au Gratin
Ingredients: ["7 each potatoes maine russet, medium, parboiled, peeled, and thinly sliced", "2 1/2 tablespoons butter unsalted", "1 clove garlic crushed", "2 each shallots or green onions, minced", "2 tablespoons flour, unbleached all-purpose", "1 1/2 cups milk at room temperature", "1 cup buttermilk at room temp", "1 teaspoon white pepper", "1/4 cup mayonnaise", "1 teaspoon dijon mustard", "1/4 teaspoon worcestershire sauce", "1/4 cup parsley leaves fresh, chopped", "2 ounces blue cheese crumbled, divided", "3 cups mushrooms raw, sliced", "1 cup monterey jack cheese grated", "1 1/2 cups potato chips coarsely crushed", "10 ounces broccoli, frozen thawed, chopped", "1 tablespoon pimentos canned, diced"]
Directions: ["Arrange half of the potatoes in the bottom of a buttered 2 1/2-quart shallow casserole dish.", "Make the buttermilk-blue cheese sauce as follows: melt butter in a medium saucepan over low heat.", "Add garlic and shallots and saute for 1 minute.", "Add flour, stir, and cook for 3 minutes more.", "Pour in milk and buttermilk all at once.", "Cook, stirring constantly, until sauce thickens and bubbles.", "Remove from heat and stir in white pepper, mayonnaise, mustard, Worcestershire, parsley and half of the blue cheese.", "Layer all the mushrooms over the potatoes in the casserole; top with half of the sauce and distribute the grated jack cheese over the sauce.", "Layer remaining potatoes over cheese and spoon remaining sauce on top.", "Sprinkle with remaining blue cheese.", "Bake at 350F (180C) for 45 minutes.", "Sprinkle potato chips over top and bake an additional 10 minutes.", "Meanwhile, blanch the broccoli.", "Arrange broccoli around outer edges of casserole and garnish with pimento; bake 5 minutes longer."]
Requirement: Lupin-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Dish Name:** Buttermilk Blue Potatoes Au Gratin (Lupin-Free)

**Modified Recipe:**

Ingredients:
- 7 each potatoes Maine russet, medium, parboiled, peeled, and thinly sliced
- 2 1/2 tablespoons unsalted butter (ensure no lupin cross-contact in processing)
- 1 clove garlic, crushed
- 2 each shallots or green onions, minced
- 2 tablespoons flour, unbleached all-purpose (ensure lupin-free)
- 1 1/2 cups milk at room temperature
- 1 cup buttermilk at room temperature
- 1 teaspoon white pepper
- 1/4 cup mayonnaise (ensure lupin-free)
- 1 teaspoon Dijon mustard (ensure lupin-free)
- 1/4 teaspoon Worcestershire sauce (ensure lupin-free)
- 1/4 cup fresh parsley leaves, chopped
- 2 ounces blue cheese, crumbled, divided
- 3 cups raw mushrooms, sliced
- 1 cup Monterey Jack cheese, grated
- 1 1/2 cups potato chips, coarsely crushed (ensure lupin-free)
- 10 ounces broccoli, frozen, thawed, chopped
- 1 tablespoon canned pimentos, diced

Instructions:
1. Preheat oven to 350°F (180°C).
2. Arrange half of the parboiled potato slices in the bottom of a buttered 2 1/2-quart shallow casserole dish.
3. To make the buttermilk-blue cheese sauce, melt butter in a medium saucepan over low heat.
4. Add garlic and shallots, sauté for 1 minute.
5. Add flour, stir, and cook for 3 minutes.
6. Pour in milk and buttermilk all at once, cook, stirring constantly, until sauce thickens and bubbles.
7. Remove from heat and stir in white pepper, mayonnaise, mustard, Worcestershire sauce, parsley, and half of the blue cheese.
8. Layer all the mushrooms over the potatoes in the casserole, top with half of the sauce, and sprinkle grated Monterey Jack cheese over the sauce.
9. Layer the remaining potato slices over the cheese and spoon the remaining sauce on top.
10. Sprinkle with the remaining blue cheese.
11. Bake for 45 minutes.
12. Sprinkle the crushed potato chips over the top and bake for an additional 10 minutes.
13. Meanwhile, blanch the broccoli.
14. Arrange broccoli around the outer edges of the casserole and garnish with pimento; bake 5 minutes longer.
```

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

- Ensure that all ingredients like unsalted butter, flour, mayonnaise, Dijon mustard, Worcestershire sauce, and potato chips are explicitly certified lupin-free, as lupin can often be present due to cross-contamination during manufacturing.
- Cross-contamination risks should be addressed explicitly, especially for processed items like flour and potato chips, which may often share facilities with lupin processing. Each ingredient must be vetted to confirm absence of lupin.

Case 124-Title: Raspberry Sponge
Ingredients: ["1/2 pint raspberries", "2/3 C sugar", "3 Tbsp lemon juice", "1 envelope gelatin", "3 Tbsp cold water", "1/2 C boiling water", "1 C whipping cream (whipped)"]
Directions: ["Mix gelatin and cold water.", "Then add boiling water."]
Requirement: Gluten-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Modified Recipe: Raspberry Sponge (Gluten-Free)**

**Ingredients:**

- 1/2 pint raspberries
- 2/3 C sugar
- 3 Tbsp lemon juice
- 1 envelope gelatin (ensure it is labeled gluten-free)
- 3 Tbsp cold water
- 1/2 C boiling water
- 1 C coconut cream (whipped)

**Directions:**

1. In a small bowl, sprinkle the gluten-free gelatin over the cold water and let it sit for a few minutes to bloom.
2. Add the boiling water to the gelatin mixture and stir until the gelatin is completely dissolved.
3. In a blender or food processor, purée the raspberries with the sugar and lemon juice until smooth.
4. Pour the raspberry mixture into a large mixing bowl.
5. Stir in the gelatin mixture until thoroughly combined.
6. Gently fold in the whipped coconut cream until the mixture is uniform in color and texture.
7. Pour the mixture into a mold or serving dish and refrigerate until set, about 4 hours or overnight.
8. Once set, serve chilled, optionally garnishing with additional raspberries or mint leaves for decoration.
```

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

The modified recipe claims to be gluten-free. However, it is important to ensure the following:

1. The envelope of gelatin must be explicitly labeled as gluten-free. Gelatin itself is usually gluten-free, but cross-contamination can occur during manufacturing unless certified.

2. The coconut cream must be free of added ingredients that might contain gluten. Some coconut creams contain stabilizers or thickeners that are not gluten-free. Ensure it is certified gluten-free.

Check these points to confirm the gluten-free status. If both ingredients are verified as gluten-free, the recipe is valid.

Case 125-Title: Vegetable Barley Soup
Ingredients: ["3 cups water", "12 cup pearl barley", "14 ounce dried porcini mushrooms", "12 cup boiling water", "2 tablespoons olive oil", "2 stalks celery, thinly sliced", "2 carrots, thinly sliced", "1 large onion, chopped", "12 ounces cremini mushrooms, thinly sliced", "2 sprigs fresh thyme", "6 cups vegetable stock or 6 cups beef stock", "2 tablespoons dry sherry", "1 teaspoon salt", "14 teaspoon fresh ground black pepper", "2 teaspoons red wine vinegar", "14 cup minced fresh flat-leaf parsley", "parmesan cheese, curls"]
Directions: ["In a saucepan, bring water and barley to a simmer over medium heat; simmer, uncovered, until almost tender, 10-15 minutes; drain and set aside.", "Meanwhile, in a small bowl, soak porcini mushrooms in boiling water until softened, about 30 minutes.", "Using a slotted spoon, gently lift mushrooms from liquid and swish in a bowl of cold water to remove any clinging sand or dirt; chop and set aside.", "Pour mushroom liquid through a sieve lined with a coffee filter into a small bowl and set aside.", "In a big pot, heat oil over medium heat; add in celery, carrots, and onion; saute until golden, 6-8 minutes.", "Add in cremini and porcini mushrooms; saute until mushrooms have released their liquid and are browned, about 10 minutes.", "Add in thyme, stock, reserved mushroom liquid, sherry, barley, salt, and pepper; bring to a boil.", "Decrease heat and simmer, stirring occasionally, until vegetables and barley are tender, 10-15 minutes.", "Taste and adjust seasoning with salt and pepper, if needed.", "Ladle into heated bowls and garnish with parsley and cheese curls."]
Requirement: Mustard-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Dish Name:** Vegetable Barley Soup (Modified)

**Ingredients:**
- 3 cups water
- 1/2 cup pearl barley
- 1/4 ounce dried porcini mushrooms
- 1/2 cup boiling water
- 2 tablespoons olive oil (ensure it's pure olive oil without additives)
- 2 stalks celery, thinly sliced
- 2 carrots, thinly sliced
- 1 large onion, chopped
- 12 ounces cremini mushrooms, thinly sliced
- 2 sprigs fresh thyme
- 6 cups vegetable stock (ensure it's mustard-free)
- 2 tablespoons dry sherry (verify it's mustard-free)
- 1 teaspoon salt
- 1/4 teaspoon fresh ground black pepper
- 2 teaspoons red wine vinegar (verify it's mustard-free)
- 1/4 cup minced fresh flat-leaf parsley
- Parmesan cheese curls (optional and ensure it's mustard-free)

**Instructions:**
1. In a saucepan, bring water and barley to a simmer over medium heat; simmer, uncovered, until almost tender, 10-15 minutes; drain and set aside.
2. Meanwhile, in a small bowl, soak porcini mushrooms in boiling water until softened, about 30 minutes.
3. Using a slotted spoon, gently lift mushrooms from liquid and swish in a bowl of cold water to remove any clinging sand or dirt; chop and set aside.
4. Pour mushroom liquid through a sieve lined with a coffee filter into a small bowl and set aside.
5. In a big pot, heat olive oil over medium heat; add in celery, carrots, and onion; sauté until golden, 6-8 minutes.
6. Add in cremini and porcini mushrooms; sauté until mushrooms have released their liquid and are browned, about 10 minutes.
7. Add in thyme, vegetable stock, reserved mushroom liquid, sherry, barley, salt, and pepper; bring to a boil.
8. Decrease heat and simmer, stirring occasionally, until vegetables and barley are tender, 10-15 minutes.
9. Taste and adjust seasoning with salt and pepper, if needed.
10. Ladle into heated bowls and garnish with parsley and cheese curls. 
```

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

Points to watch out:

1. Ingredient Safety:
   - Ensure the vegetable stock, dry sherry, red wine vinegar, and Parmesan cheese used are certified mustard-free. The modified recipe specifies verifying these ingredients for absence of mustard, but unless there is explicit certification or labeling confirming they are mustard-free, there is a potential risk of mustard presence or cross-contamination.

2. Requirement Fulfillment:
   - Verify that any olive oil additives, if any, do not contain mustard or have been cross-contaminated with mustard products.

Ensure these precautions are taken to safely meet the mustard-free requirement.

```markdown
**Modified Homemade Sweet And Sour Sauce (Gluten-Free)**

**Ingredients:**
- 1/4 cup ketchup (ensure gluten-free brand)
- 1/4 cup brown sugar
- 1/4 cup water
- 2 tablespoons white vinegar
- 1 tablespoon tamari (gluten-free soy sauce alternative)
```

Ingredients: ["2 whole Ripe Bananas, Mashed Until Creamy", "1/3 cups Peanut Butter, Creamy Or Chunky", "2/3 cups Unsweetened Applesauce", "1/4 cups Vanilla Whey Protein Powder", "1 teaspoon Vanilla Extract", "1 teaspoon Butter Extract (optional)", "1-1/2 cup Quick Oatmeal, Uncooked", "1/4 cups Chopped Peanuts", "1/4 cups Carob Chips Or Chocolate Chips (optional)"]
Directions: ["Preheat heat oven to 350\u00b0F.", "In a large bowl, mix mashed banana and peanut butter until completely combined. Then add in the applesauce, vanilla protein powder and vanilla and butter extracts. Mix again until completely combined.", "Add in the oatmeal and nuts to the banana mixture and combine. (Add the optional carob/chocolate chips at this time if you want them mixed throughout.)", "Let dough rest for 10 minutes.", "Drop cookie dough, by spoonfuls, onto a parchment paper lined cookie sheet and flatten cookies into circles, about a 1/3\" thick. (If you want the optional carob/chocolate chips on the top of the cookies, push them into the cookies now.)", "Bake cookies approximately 30 minutes, or until golden brown and done. Requirement: Fish-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Modified Recipe: Peanut Butter Banana Oat Breakfast Cookies With Carob/Chocolate Chips**

**Ingredients:**
- 2 ripe bananas, mashed until creamy
- 1/3 cup sunflower seed butter, creamy or chunky
- 2/3 cup unsweetened applesauce
- 1/4 cup vanilla plant-based protein powder
- 1 teaspoon vanilla extract
- 1 teaspoon butter-flavored extract (optional)
- 1 1/2 cups quick oats, uncooked
- 1/4 cup chopped sunflower seeds
- 1/4 cup carob chips or dairy-free chocolate chips (optional)

**Directions:**
1. Preheat the oven to 350°F.
2. In a large bowl, mix the mashed bananas and sunflower seed butter until completely combined. Add the applesauce, vanilla protein powder, vanilla extract, and butter-flavored extract. Mix again until fully combined.
3. Add the oatmeal and chopped sunflower seeds to the banana mixture and combine thoroughly. If using carob or chocolate chips and want them throughout, add them now.
4. Let the dough rest for 10 minutes.
5. Drop cookie dough by spoonfuls onto a parchment-lined cookie sheet and flatten into circles, about 1/3" thick. If you want carob/chocolate chips on top, press them into the cookies at this stage.
6. Bake the cookies for approximately 30 minutes, or until golden brown and done. Remove from the oven and let them rest on the cookie sheet for 5 minutes, then transfer to a cooling rack.
7. If desired, use a pizza cutter or sharp knife to score the tops of the warm cookies to create fork tine marks.
8. Once the cookies are completely cool, store them in a covered container. Enjoy!
```

```markdown
- 8 (1/2-inch) slices kasseri cheese (about 1 1/2 ounces each)
- Salt
- Freshly ground black pepper
- 2 cups brandy, or enough to cover cheese slices
- 1 cup certified peanut-free all-purpose flour
- 4 tablespoons butter
- 3 to 4 tablespoons lemon juice
- 4 rounds of pita bread, brushed with olive oil (made from olive or grapeseed oil), grilled and quartered
- 1 cup kalamata olives

**Instructions:**
1. Season both sides of the kasseri cheese with salt and freshly ground black pepper.
2. Place the cheese in a shallow dish and cover with brandy.
3. Cover with plastic wrap and refrigerate for 2 hours.
4. Season the peanut-free flour with salt and freshly ground black pepper.
5. Remove the cheese from the dish, reserving 1/4 cup of the brandy, and dredge in the seasoned flour, coating completely.
6. In a large sauté pan over medium heat, melt the butter.
7. Pan-fry the cheese for 2 minutes on each side.
8. Add the reserved brandy and carefully flame the liquor, shaking the pan back and forth several times.
9. Add the lemon juice, to taste.
10. Remove from the pan and serve immediately with the grilled pita bread and kalamata olives.
```

Case 135-Title: Brown Sugar Brownies
Ingredients: ["2 sticks margarine", "1 lb. light brown sugar plus 1 c. white sugar", "4 eggs", "3 c. self-rising flour", "1 tsp. vanilla"]
Directions: ["Do not use whisk or mixer!", "In saucepan put margarine and sugar.", "Stir over medium heat until it simmers.", "Remove from heat and cool.", "Add well beaten eggs, a small amount at a time.", "Add flour and vanilla.", "Mix well and pour into a well-greased and floured 12 x 16-inch pan or two smaller ones.", "Bake at 350\u00b0 for 30 to 35 minutes.", "Cut in 1-inch squares while still warm."]
Requirement: Peanut-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Modified Recipe: Brown Sugar Brownies**

**Ingredients:**
- 1 cup unsalted butter (certified peanut-free) or butter alternative certified peanut-free
- 1 lb. light brown sugar
- 1 cup white sugar
- 4 eggs
- 3 cups all-purpose flour
- 1 tbsp baking powder
- 1/2 tsp salt
- 1 tsp vanilla extract

**Instructions:**
1. Preheat your oven to 350°F (175°C).
2. In a saucepan, melt the butter (or peanut-free butter alternative) over medium heat. Add both sugars and stir until the mixture simmers, then remove from heat and let cool.
3. Slowly add the well-beaten eggs to the cooled sugar mixture, incorporating a small amount at a time.
4. In a separate bowl, sift together the all-purpose flour, baking powder, and salt.
5. Gradually incorporate the dry ingredients into the wet mixture, stirring gently with a spatula.
6. Add the vanilla extract and mix until well combined.
7. Pour the batter into a well-greased and floured 12 x 16-inch pan or two smaller pans.
8. Bake in the preheated oven for 30 to 35 minutes, until a toothpick inserted in the center comes out clean.
9. Once done, cut the brownies into 1-inch squares while still warm.

**Note:** Ensure all ingredients, especially the butter or butter alternative, are certified peanut-free.
```

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

1. **Ingredient Safety and Cross-Contamination:** 
   - While the recipe specifies "unsalted butter (certified peanut-free) or butter alternative certified peanut-free,” it's essential to ensure that all ingredients, especially those that are prone to cross-contamination, such as flour, sugar, and other processed ingredients, are also certified peanut-free. It's crucial to verify that these ingredients are manufactured in a peanut-free facility or have a certification stating they are peanut-free.
   
2. **Sift Together Ingredients:**
   - When sifting together the all-purpose flour, baking powder, and salt, use a clean and uncontaminated sifter to prevent cross-contamination.

3. **Directional Steps Consistency:**
   - The cooking steps mentioned in the modified recipe are logical and align well with the substitution, maintaining the integrity of the steps used in traditional baking.

By ensuring all ingredients used, including processed ones, are verified to be free from cross-contamination with peanuts, the requirement can be confidently met.

```markdown
- 1 (10 ounce) can enchilada sauce, divided (ensure the brand specifies "shellfish-free")
- 1/2 teaspoon salt
- 1 1/2 pounds ground beef chuck
- 1 (10 ounce) can tomato sauce (ensure no additives derived from shellfish)
- 1 cup shredded Mexican cheese blend, divided (check ingredient list for shellfish-free assurance)
```

```markdown
### Surprise Coconut Pie (Gluten-Free)

#### Ingredients:
- 4 eggs
- 1 3/4 cups sugar
- 2 cups milk (or unsweetened almond milk for a dairy-free option)
- 1 teaspoon vanilla extract
- 1/2 cup gluten-free all-purpose flour blend (ensure it contains xanthan gum or add 1/4 teaspoon)

- 1 (7 oz.) package unsweetened flaked coconut
```

Case 143-Title: Pastrami Cupcakes
Ingredients: ["1 1/2 cups self-rising flour", "1 1/4 cups all-purpose flour", "2 sticks unsalted butter, at room temperature", "2 cups granulated sugar", "4 large eggs, at room temperature", "1 cup whole milk", "1 teaspoon vanilla extract", "3 tablespoons caraway seeds", "8 ounces pastrami, chopped", "Honey Mustard Glaze, recipe follows", "Honey Mustard Frosting, recipe follows", "Soft Pretzel, sliced in slivers, for garnish", "1/4 cup powdered sugar", "1 tablespoon honey", "1 tablespoon spicy brown mustard", "2 sticks (1/2 pound) unsalted butter, at room temperature", "1/2 cup honey mustard", "1 tablespoon spicy mustard", "2 cups powdered sugar"]
Directions: ["Preheat the oven to 350 degrees F. Line cupcake pans with 24 liners.", "In a medium bowl, combine both flours.", "Using an electric mixer with the paddle attachment, cream the butter until smooth.", "Gradually add the granulated sugar and beat until fluffy.", "Add the eggs, one at a time, beating well after each addition.", "Add the flour mixture in three parts, alternating with the milk.", "Add the vanilla.", "Scrape down the sides of the bowl to make sure all the ingredients are well blended.", "Beat until just combined.", "Do not over beat.", "Fold in the caraway seeds.", "Spoon the batter into the liners, filling the cups two-thirds full.", "Bake until a toothpick inserted in the center comes out clean, about 16 minutes.", "Cool the cupcakes completely.", "Cut the tops off the cupcakes and reserve.", "Place the chopped pastrami on the bottom half of the cupcakes.", "Drizzle 1 teaspoon Honey Mustard Glaze (more or less to taste) on the pastrami.", "Place the cupcake tops on top of the glaze, pressing down gently.", "Frost the cupcakes with Honey Mustard Buttercream Frosting.", "Garnish with soft pretzel slivers.", "In a small bowl, combine the powdered sugar, honey and mustard, and mix until smooth.", "Using an electric mixer with the paddle attachment, cream the butter until smooth.", "Add the honey mustard and spicy mustard and mix on high for 1 minute, scraping down the sides often.", "Add the powdered sugar 1/4 cup at a time, mixing well after each addition."]
Requirement: Lupin-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Modified Pastrami Cupcakes Recipe**

**Ingredients:**

- 1 1/2 cups self-rising flour (ensure it is lupin-free, check labels carefully)
- 1 1/4 cups all-purpose flour (ensure it is lupin-free, check labels carefully)
- 2 sticks unsalted butter, at room temperature
- 2 cups granulated sugar
- 4 large eggs, at room temperature
- 1 cup whole milk
- 1 teaspoon vanilla extract
- 3 tablespoons caraway seeds
- 8 ounces pastrami, chopped
- Soft pretzel, sliced in slivers, for garnish (ensure they are lupin-free)
- **Honey Mustard Glaze:**
  - 1/4 cup powdered sugar (ensure it is lupin-free)
  - 1 tablespoon honey
  - 1 tablespoon spicy brown mustard (ensure it is lupin-free, check labels carefully)
- **Honey Mustard Frosting:**
  - 2 sticks (1/2 pound) unsalted butter, at room temperature
  - 1/2 cup honey mustard (ensure lupin-free)
  - 1 tablespoon spicy mustard (ensure lupin-free, check labels carefully)
  - 2 cups powdered sugar (ensure it is lupin-free)

**Instructions:**

1. Preheat the oven to 350 degrees F. Line cupcake pans with 24 liners.
2. In a medium bowl, combine both flours.
3. Using an electric mixer with the paddle attachment, cream the butter until smooth.
4. Gradually add the granulated sugar and beat until fluffy.
5. Add the eggs, one at a time, beating well after each addition.
6. Add the flour mixture in three parts, alternating with the milk.
7. Add the vanilla extract.
8. Scrape down the sides of the bowl to ensure all the ingredients are well blended.
9. Beat until just combined. Do not over beat.
10. Fold in the caraway seeds.
11. Spoon the batter into the liners, filling the cups two-thirds full.
12. Bake until a toothpick inserted in the center comes out clean, about 16 minutes.
13. Cool the cupcakes completely.
14. Cut the tops off the cupcakes and reserve.
15. Place the chopped pastrami on the bottom half of the cupcakes.
16. Drizzle 1 teaspoon Honey Mustard Glaze (more or less to taste) on the pastrami.
17. Place the cupcake tops on top of the glaze, pressing down gently.
18. Frost the cupcakes with Honey Mustard Buttercream Frosting.
19. Garnish with soft pretzel slivers.

**Honey Mustard Glaze:**

1. In a small bowl, combine the powdered sugar, honey, and mustard, and mix until smooth.

**Honey Mustard Frosting:**

1. Using an electric mixer with the paddle attachment, cream the butter until smooth.
2. Add the honey mustard and spicy mustard and mix on high for 1 minute, scraping down the sides often.
3. Add the powdered sugar 1/4 cup at a time, mixing well after each addition.
```

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

Case 144-Title: Mashed Potato Cocoa Cake
Ingredients: ["1/2 c. butter", "2 c. sugar", "1/2 c. milk", "4 eggs", "1/2 c. cocoa", "1/2 tsp. cinnamon", "1 tsp. vanilla", "1/8 tsp. salt", "2/3 c. milk", "2 c. sifted flour", "3 tsp. baking powder", "1 c. hot mashed potatoes", "1 c. chopped nuts"]
Directions: ["Cream butter.", "Beat in sugar.", "Add beaten egg yolks, vanilla, mashed potatoes and cocoa.", "Add sifted dry ingredients alternately with milk, then add nuts.", "Fold in stiffly beaten egg whites. Bake in buttered flat cake pan for about 50 minutes in a 350\u00b0 oven."]
Requirement: Wheat-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Mashed Potato Cocoa Cake (Wheat-Free Version)**

**Ingredients:**
- 1/2 cup unsalted butter
- 2 cups granulated sugar
- 1/2 cup milk (any preferred milk alternative, e.g., almond milk or oat milk, unsweetened)
- 4 large eggs, separated
- 1/2 cup unsweetened cocoa powder
- 1/2 teaspoon ground cinnamon
- 1 teaspoon vanilla extract
- 1/8 teaspoon salt
- 2/3 cup milk (same milk alternative as above)
- 2 cups gluten-free all-purpose flour blend (ensure it contains xanthan gum or similar binding agent)
- 3 teaspoons gluten-free baking powder
- 1 cup hot mashed potatoes (ensure no added dairy if using milk alternative)
- 1 cup chopped nuts (e.g., walnuts or pecans)

**Instructions:**
1. Preheat the oven to 350°F (175°C). Butter a flat cake pan lightly or line with parchment paper.
2. In a large mixing bowl, cream together the butter and sugar until light and fluffy.
3. Beat in the egg yolks one at a time. Add vanilla extract, mashed potatoes, and cocoa powder; mix thoroughly.
4. In a separate bowl, combine the gluten-free flour, baking powder, cinnamon, and salt. Whisk to blend evenly.
5. Gradually add the sifted dry ingredients into the creamed mixture, alternating with the milk alternative. Mix until just combined.
6. Stir in the chopped nuts until evenly distributed.
7. In another bowl, beat the egg whites until stiff peaks form. Gently fold the beaten egg whites into the batter until no streaks remain.
8. Pour the batter into the prepared cake pan and smooth the top with a spatula.
9. Bake in the preheated oven for approximately 50 minutes or until a toothpick inserted in the center comes out clean.
10. Let the cake cool in the pan for 10 minutes, then turn out onto a wire rack to cool completely before serving.
```

Case 145-Title: Chinese Sesame Chicken With Celery Salad
Ingredients: ["4 teaspoons sesame seeds", "3 chicken breasts", "1 teaspoon five-spice powder", "2 teaspoons light soy sauce", "3 stalks celery", "1/2 teaspoon ground ginger", "4 teaspoons sesame oil", "4 teaspoons light soy sauce", "4 teaspoons olive oil"]
Directions: ["Toast sesame seeds on shallow baking tray at 350F for 5 minutes. Alternatively, you may buy toasted sesame seeds from supermarkets.", "Place water and chicken in pan. Make sure chicken is well covered with water.", "Add spice powder and soy sauce before bringing slowly to boil. Simmer over low fire, covered until chicken is just cooked.", "When chicken has cooled, cut into slices.", "Chop celery diagonally and boil in chicken broth for a minute. Towel dry celery to remove excess moisture from celery.", "Combine rest of ingredients and mix well with chicken and celery. Serve with sesame seeds."]
Requirement: Egg-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Modified Recipe: Chinese Sesame Chicken With Celery Salad**

**Ingredients:**
- 4 teaspoons toasted sesame seeds
- 3 chicken breasts
- 1 teaspoon Chinese five-spice powder
- 2 teaspoons tamari (gluten-free soy sauce)
- 3 stalks celery
- 1/2 teaspoon freshly grated ginger
- 4 teaspoons toasted sesame oil
- 4 teaspoons tamari
- 4 teaspoons olive oil

**Directions:**
1. Preheat your oven to 350°F (175°C). Spread sesame seeds on a shallow baking tray and toast for 5 minutes, or use pre-toasted sesame seeds.
2. Place the chicken in a pan and cover it with water. Add the five-spice powder and tamari. Bring slowly to a boil, then lower to a simmer. Cover and cook until the chicken is just done.
3. Once cooked, remove the chicken from the broth and allow it to cool. Slice the chicken into pieces.
4. Diagonally chop the celery sticks. Boil the chopped celery in the chicken broth for 1 minute, then towel dry to remove excess moisture.
5. In a large bowl, combine the toasted sesame oil, tamari, olive oil, and grated ginger. Mix well.
6. Toss the sliced chicken and celery in the prepared dressing until well coated.
7. Serve with toasted sesame seeds sprinkled on top.
```

Case 146-Title: Martha Stewart'S Slow-Cooker Persian Lamb Stew
Ingredients: ["1 lamb shoulder (4 to 5 pounds)", "Coarse salt and freshly ground pepper", "2 tablespoons extra-virgin olive oil", "2 large onions, finely chopped", "2 large carrots, finely chopped", "2 celery stalks, finely chopped", "1 teaspoon dried dill weed", "1 head garlic, cloves peeled", "3 thyme sprigs", "1 cup dry white wine", "1 cup fresh orange juice", "1 dried lime", "1 large pinch saffron threads", "Cooked quinoa, for serving", "Coarsely chopped fresh dill, pomegranate seeds, and unsalted pistachios, for garnish"]
Directions: ["Preheat a 5-to 6-quart slow cooker.", "Season lamb with salt and pepper. In a large Dutch oven, heat oil over medium-high. Add lamb and cook until golden brown all over, about 8 minutes. Transfer to the slow cooker.", "Add onions, carrots, celery, and dill weed to Dutch oven and cook, stirring often, until vegetables are tender, 6 to 8 minutes. Transfer to slow cooker. Add garlic, thyme, wine, orange juice, dried lime, and saffron. Cover and cook on low, until meat is falling apart and shreds easily, 7 to 8 hours (or on high for 5 to 6 hours). Skim fat from surface. Serve stew over quinoa, topped with dill, pomegranate seeds, and pistachios."]
Requirement: Celery-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Modified Recipe:**

Ingredients:
- 1 lamb shoulder (4 to 5 pounds)
- Coarse salt and freshly ground pepper
- 2 tablespoons extra-virgin olive oil
- 2 large onions, finely chopped
- 2 large carrots, finely chopped
- 2 parsnips, finely chopped (substitute for celery)
- 1 teaspoon dried dill weed
- 1 head garlic, cloves peeled
- 3 thyme sprigs
- 1 cup dry white wine
- 1 cup fresh orange juice
- 1 dried lime
- 1 large pinch saffron threads
- Cooked quinoa, for serving
- Coarsely chopped fresh dill, pomegranate seeds, and unsalted pistachios, for garnish

Directions:
1. Preheat a 5-to 6-quart slow cooker.
2. Season lamb with salt and pepper. In a large Dutch oven, heat oil over medium-high. Add lamb and cook until golden brown all over, about 8 minutes. Transfer to the slow cooker.
3. Add onions, carrots, parsnips, and dill weed to the Dutch oven and cook, stirring often, until vegetables are tender, 6 to 8 minutes. Transfer to the slow cooker.
4. Add garlic, thyme, wine, orange juice, dried lime, and saffron. Cover and cook on low, until meat is falling apart and shreds easily, 7 to 8 hours (or on high for 5 to 6 hours). Skim fat from surface.
5. Serve stew over quinoa, topped with dill, pomegranate seeds, and pistachios.
```

Case 147-Title: Emeril's Corn Tortillas
Ingredients: ["2 cups corn flour", "1 teaspoon salt", "2 tablespoons lard", "1 1/2 cups water"]
Directions: ["In a mixing bowl, combine the flour, salt, and lard.", "Mix well.", "Stir in the water.", "**The dough should be slightly wet.", "Form the dough into a smooth ball.", "Divide the dough into 12 pieces.", "Place a little water on the hands and form the dough into small balls.", "Place the balls on a piece of parchment paper (12 inches by 8 1/2 inches).", "Using your hands, flatten the dough and form into a flat circle.", "Place a piece of plastic wrap over the circle.", "Using a rolling pin, roll the dough out into a 6 1/2 to 7 inch circle and 1/8 inch thick.", "In a medium non-stick skillet, over medium heat, brown the tortillas for 1 to 2 minutes on each side.", "Remove and place between two sheets of parchment paper.", "Repeat the above process with the remaining dough.", "Serve warm."]
Requirement: Soy-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Modified Recipe: Emeril's Corn Tortillas**

**Ingredients:**
- 2 cups corn flour (masa harina)
- 1 teaspoon salt
- 2 tablespoons coconut oil (ensure it is soy-free)
- 1 1/2 cups water

**Directions:**
1. In a mixing bowl, combine the corn flour, salt, and coconut oil.
2. Mix well with your hands until the consistency resembles wet sand.
3. Gradually stir in the water, mixing continuously until the dough is slightly wet.
4. Form the dough into a smooth ball.
5. Divide the dough into 12 equal pieces.
6. Place a little water on your hands and form each piece into a small ball.
7. Place each ball on a piece of parchment paper (12 inches by 8 1/2 inches).
8. Using your hands, flatten each ball into a flat circle.
9. Place a piece of plastic wrap over the circle.
10. Use a rolling pin to roll the dough out to a 6 1/2 to 7-inch circle, approximately 1/8 inch thick.
11. In a medium non-stick skillet over medium heat, brown each tortilla for 1 to 2 minutes on each side until they have light brown specks.
12. Remove the tortillas and place them between two sheets of parchment paper to keep them warm and soft.
13. Repeat the process with the remaining dough.
14. Serve warm.
```

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

- **Ingredient Safety**: The modified recipe uses coconut oil, which is typically soy-free. However, for the soy-free requirement, it is crucial that the coconut oil used is explicitly labeled as soy-free to avoid cross-contamination risks. Without explicit certification, there's a potential risk of soy contamination. Please ensure the coconut oil used is verified and certified as soy-free.

```markdown
**Modified Recipe: Death By Chocolate (Sesame-Free)**

**Ingredients:**
- **Cake:** 1 recipe chocolate cake (homemade or use a boxed mix labeled sesame-free)
- **Optional:** 1 cup coffee or espresso (as a substitute for Kahlua)
- **Mousse:** 4 boxes chocolate mousse mix (ensure it's sesame-free or make homemade chocolate mousse)
- **Whipped Topping:** 2 (12 oz.) tubs whipped topping (ensure it's sesame-free, such as TruWhip or homemade whipped cream)
- **Topping:** 6 chocolate-covered toffee bars (ensure they're sesame-free, such as Heath bars)

**Directions:**
1. **Bake Cake:** Prepare the chocolate cake according to the recipe or package instructions in a 9 x 13-inch pan.
2. **Soak Cake:** Allow the cake to cool slightly. Prick the top with a fork and pour coffee or espresso over the cake. Let it soak in overnight.
3. **Prepare Mousse:** Prepare the chocolate mousse according to package directions or make homemade mousse.
4. **Assemble Dessert:**
   - Crumble 1/3 of the soaked cake and place it at the bottom of a glass bowl.
   - Layer 1/3 of the chocolate mousse over the cake.
   - Add 1/3 of the whipped topping.
   - Sprinkle 2 crumbled chocolate-covered toffee bars over the whipped topping.

5. **Repeat Layers:** Continue layering with the remaining 2/3 of the ingredients (cake, mousse, whipped topping, and toffee bars) to create a trifle.

6. **Chill and Serve:** Chill the dessert in the refrigerator for at least 2 hours before serving to allow flavors to meld.

```

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

- Ingredient safety is paramount with sesame allergies; cross-contamination from processing facilities needs verification.

Requirement: Peanut-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Dish Name:** Red and Blue Corn Sticks (Peanut-Free)

**Ingredients:**
- 4 tablespoons unsalted butter, melted
- 1 cup red or blue cornmeal
- 1 cup all-purpose flour
- 3 tablespoons sugar
- 4 teaspoons baking powder
- 1/2 teaspoon salt
- 1 1/4 cups milk
- 1 large egg

**Instructions:**
1. Preheat the oven to 425 degrees Fahrenheit.
2. Brush 12 iron corn stick molds generously with some of the melted butter, and set aside.
3. In a medium-size bowl, combine the cornmeal, flour, sugar, baking powder, and salt.
4. In a small bowl, whisk together the milk, egg, and remaining melted butter.
5. Stir the milk mixture into the cornmeal mixture just until moistened; the mixture will be a bit lumpy.
6. Spread the mixture into the prepared molds, nearly filling them.
7. Bake in the preheated oven until puffed and lightly browned, about 20 minutes. A toothpick inserted in the center should come out clean.
8. Serve warm.
```

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

- Ingredient Safety: While the recipe indicates that it is peanut-free, the caution arises from the lack of explicit certification for ingredient safety concerning potential cross-contamination with peanuts. Ingredients such as cornmeal, flour, and baking powder should be verified to ensure they are processed in a peanut-free facility or are explicitly labeled as peanut-free to avoid any cross-contamination risks.

Case 155-Title: Macaroon Bars
Ingredients: ["1 stick butter", "1 c. sugar", "2 eggs, separated", "1 c. flour", "1/4 tsp. salt", "1 1/2 c. coconut", "1/2 c. chopped pecans", "2 tsp. lemon rind", "1/4 tsp. cream of tartar", "1 Tbsp. lemon juice"]
Directions: ["Cream butter and 1/2 cup sugar.", "Beat in egg yolks, one at a time.", "Gently beat in flour and salt.", "Stir in 1 cup of coconut, nuts and rind.", "Spread in 13 x 9-inch pan. Bake at 350\u00b0 for 20 minutes or golden brown on edges.", "Beat egg whites; add cream of tartar until foamy throughout.", "Gradually add remaining sugar, beating after each addition.", "Beat in juice and beat until stiff peaks.", "Spread over cooled mixture.", "Sprinkle with remaining coconut.", "Bake at 375\u00b0 until topping is golden brown, 10 to 15 minutes.", "Cool and cut into bars.", "Store in tightly covered box."]
Requirement: Shellfish-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Dish Name:** Macaroon Bars (Shellfish-Free)

**Modified Recipe:**

**Ingredients:**
- 1 stick unsalted butter
- 1 cup granulated sugar
- 2 large eggs, separated
- 1 cup all-purpose flour
- 1/4 tsp sea salt
- 1 1/2 cups shredded unsweetened coconut
- 1/2 cup chopped pecans
- 2 tsp finely grated lemon zest
- 1/4 tsp cream of tartar
- 1 Tbsp freshly squeezed lemon juice

**Directions:**
1. Preheat oven to 350°F (175°C).
2. In a mixing bowl, cream the butter and 1/2 cup of the granulated sugar until light and fluffy.
3. Beat in egg yolks, one at a time, ensuring each is fully incorporated before adding the next.
4. Gradually add the flour and sea salt to the mixture, and mix until just combined.
5. Stir in 1 cup of shredded coconut, chopped pecans, and lemon zest.
6. Spread the mixture evenly in a 13 x 9-inch baking pan.
7. Bake for 20 minutes, or until the edges are golden brown.
8. While the base is cooling, increase oven temperature to 375°F (190°C).
9. In a clean bowl, beat the egg whites with the cream of tartar until foamy.
10. Gradually add the remaining 1/2 cup of granulated sugar, continuing to beat until stiff peaks form.
11. Gently fold in the lemon juice.
12. Spread the egg white mixture evenly over the cooled base.
13. Sprinkle the remaining 1/2 cup of shredded coconut over the top.
14. Return to the oven and bake for an additional 10 to 15 minutes, or until the topping is golden brown.
15. Allow to cool completely in the pan.
16. Cut into bars and store in an airtight container.
```

```markdown
**Modified Pecan Pie Recipe:**

- 1/2 cup coconut sugar
- 1/2 cup maple syrup
- 1/4 teaspoon salt
- 1 tablespoon all-purpose flour (or gluten-free flour for gluten-free option)
- 3 eggs
- 1 tablespoon unsalted butter or dairy-free butter
- 1 teaspoon pure vanilla extract
- 1 cup pecans

**Instructions:**
```

Case 160-Title: Spicy Vegetable Fritters
Ingredients: ["2 teaspoons oil, plus more for deep-frying", "1 cup gram flour (chickpea)", "1 teaspoon cumin seed, lightly crushed", "1 teaspoon coriander seed, lightly crushed", "1/2 teaspoon cayenne pepper", "1/2 teaspoon minced garlic", "1/2 teaspoon salt", "1/4 teaspoon baking powder", "1/4 teaspoon ajwain seed, lightly crushed (optional)", "1 cup water, approximately", "1 lb mixed vegetables, trimmed and cut into bite-size pieces (such as cauliflower, zucchini, shiitake mushrooms, onion, and/or green beans)", "chutney, for serving"]
Directions: ["Pour oil to a depth of 3 to 4 inches into a deep-fryer or a large, heavy saucepan and heat over medium-high heat to 350F.", "(The oil should come no more than halfway up the sides of the pan.) While the oil is heating, prepare the batter.", "Combine the flour, 2 tsp oil, cumin, coriander, cayenne, garlic, salt, baking powder, and ajwain (if using) in a medium bowl.", "While stirring, gradually pour in enough water to make a batter of coating consistency.", "Working in batches, dip the vegetable pieces into the batter, letting the excess drip back into the bowl, then carefully lower the coated vegetables into the hot oil.", "Do not crowd the pan.", "Fry until golden brown, 2 to 3 minutes.", "Remove the fritters from the oil with tongs or a slotted spoon and drain on paper towels.", "Continue with the remaining vegetables, allowing the oil to reheat between batches as needed.", "Arrange the fritters on a warmed platter and serve immediately with chutney alongside for dipping."]
Requirement: Gluten-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
### Modified Recipe: Spicy Vegetable Fritters (Gluten-Free)

#### Ingredients
- 2 teaspoons oil, plus more for deep-frying (use a high smoke point oil like avocado or sunflower)
- 1 cup chickpea flour (gram flour)
- 1 teaspoon cumin seeds, lightly crushed
- 1 teaspoon coriander seeds, lightly crushed
- 1/2 teaspoon cayenne pepper
- 1/2 teaspoon minced garlic
- 1/2 teaspoon salt
- 1/4 teaspoon gluten-free baking powder
- 1/4 teaspoon ajwain seeds, lightly crushed (optional)
- 1 cup water, approximately
- 1 lb mixed vegetables, trimmed and cut into bite-size pieces (such as cauliflower, zucchini, shiitake mushrooms, onion, and/or green beans)
- Gluten-free chutney, for serving

#### Directions
1. Pour oil to a depth of 3 to 4 inches into a deep-fryer or a large, heavy saucepan and heat over medium-high heat to 350°F. (The oil should come no more than halfway up the sides of the pan.)
2. While the oil is heating, prepare the batter: In a medium bowl, combine chickpea flour, 2 teaspoons oil, cumin seeds, coriander seeds, cayenne, garlic, salt, gluten-free baking powder, and ajwain seeds (if using).
3. Gradually pour in enough water while stirring to achieve a coating-consistent batter.
4. Working in batches, dip the vegetable pieces into the batter, allowing excess to drip back into the bowl.
5. Carefully lower the coated vegetables into the hot oil. Do not crowd the pan.
6. Fry until golden brown, about 2 to 3 minutes.
7. Remove the fritters from the oil with tongs or a slotted spoon and drain on paper towels.
8. Continue with the remaining vegetables, allowing oil to reheat between batches as needed.
9. Arrange the fritters on a warmed platter and serve immediately with gluten-free chutney alongside for dipping.
```

```markdown
**Modified Zucchini Squares Recipe**

- 4 eggs, beaten
- 1/2 cup sunflower oil or olive oil
- 1 cup gluten-free all-purpose flour
- 3 cups zucchini, unpeeled and sliced
- 1/2 cup onion, finely chopped
- 1/2 cup nutritional yeast
- 2 tablespoons parsley, chopped
```

```markdown
**Modified Chocolate Chip Cookies Recipe**

**Ingredients:**
- 1 cup packed brown sugar
- 2/3 cup coconut oil, softened
- 1 flax egg (1 tablespoon ground flaxseed mixed with 2.5 tablespoons water, let sit for 5 minutes before use)
- 1 teaspoon vanilla extract
- 1 1/2 cups all-purpose flour (confirmed lupin-free)
- 1/2 teaspoon baking soda
- 1/2 teaspoon salt
- 6 ounces allergy-safe, certified lupin-free chocolate chips

**Directions:**

5. Fold in the certified lupin-free chocolate chips gently.
6. Drop the dough by rounded teaspoonfuls about 2 inches apart onto an ungreased cookie sheet.
```

Case 163-Title: Roasted Tomatoes with Mushrooms
Ingredients: ["1 pints cherry tomatoes - washed and halved", "4 oz baby portabello mushrooms - wiped clean and quartered", "2 tbsp extra virgin olive oil", "2 tbsp balsamic vinegar", "3/4 tsp dried rosemary", "1/2 tsp dried oregano", "1/2 tsp dried basil", "1 salt and pepper to taste"]
Directions: ["Preheat oven to 400F.", "Line a baking sheet with aluminum foil and set aside.", "Rinse cherry tomatoes under cold, running water.", "Cut each in half from stem to \"butt\" and place in a large bowl.", "Wipe mushrooms clean with a slightly dampened, clean dish towel.", "Cut each mushroom in half lengthwise, then cut each half in half lengthwise again.", "Place in bowl with tomatoes.", "In a small bowl whisk together all your other ingredients.", "Pour over your tomatoes and mushrooms.", "Toss gently to coat.", "Pour out onto baking sheet and spread out into an even, single layer.", "Place in oven and bake 15-20 minutes or until tomatoes are looking \"wilty\" mushrooms are soft."]
Requirement: Peanut-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Modified Recipe for Roasted Tomatoes with Mushrooms**

**Ingredients:**
- 1 pint cherry tomatoes - washed and halved
- 4 oz baby portobello mushrooms - wiped clean and quartered
- 2 tbsp extra virgin olive oil (ensure peanut-free)
- 2 tbsp balsamic vinegar
- 3/4 tsp dried rosemary
- 1/2 tsp dried oregano
- 1/2 tsp dried basil
- Salt and pepper to taste

**Directions:**
1. Preheat oven to 400°F.
2. Line a baking sheet with aluminum foil and set aside.
3. Rinse cherry tomatoes under cold, running water.
4. Cut each in half from stem to "butt" and place in a large bowl.
5. Wipe mushrooms clean with a slightly dampened, clean dish towel.
6. Cut each mushroom in half lengthwise, then cut each half in half lengthwise again.
7. Place mushrooms in the bowl with the tomatoes.
8. In a small bowl, whisk together olive oil, balsamic vinegar, rosemary, oregano, basil, salt, and pepper.
9. Pour the dressing over the tomatoes and mushrooms.
10. Toss gently to coat the vegetables evenly.
11. Pour the coated vegetables onto the prepared baking sheet and spread them out into an even, single layer.
12. Place in oven and bake for 15-20 minutes or until the tomatoes are looking "wilty" and the mushrooms are soft.
```

Case 164-Title: Shepherd Pie
Ingredients: ["1 1/2 lbs lean ground beef", "1 cup diced carrot", "1/2 cup diced celery", "1/4 cup diced onion", "1 cup diced green beans (I used fresh but you can use frozen or canned)", "1/4 teaspoon black pepper", "1/2 teaspoon granulated garlic", "1 1/2 cups prepared beef gravy", "2 1/2 cups mashed potatoes", "1/2 cup shredded monterey jack and cheddar cheese blend"]
Directions: ["Scramble the ground beef in a large skillet.", "Add the onions, celery, green beans and carrots and heat for about three minutes.", "Sprinkle the black pepper and granulated garlic over the mixture and stir inches.", "Continue heating on medium-low heat until the veggies start to soften.", "I cooked about 10 to 12 minutes.", "Add the prepared brown gravy and stir.", "Mixture should be thick. If the mixture is runny add 1 TBS of flour and stir in and heat till bubbly.", "Remove from heat and pour into a casserole dish sprayed with a cooking spray.", "Pour the meat and veggie mixture into the dish.", "Top by spoonfuls with the mashed potatoes. Requirement: Egg-free

The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Modified Shepherd's Pie Recipe (Egg-Free)**

**Ingredients:**
- 1 1/2 lbs ground beef (or ground turkey for a lighter variant)
- 1 cup diced carrot
- 1/2 cup diced celery
- 1/4 cup diced onion
- 1 cup diced green beans (fresh or frozen)
- 1/4 teaspoon black pepper
- 1/2 teaspoon granulated garlic
- 1 1/2 cups prepared beef or vegetable gravy (ensure it is egg-free)
- 2 1/2 cups mashed potatoes (prepared with dairy or non-dairy milk and butter substitutes, ensuring all components are egg-free)
- 1/2 cup shredded dairy-free cheese blend (or use any non-dairy cheese suitable for melting)

**Directions:**
1. Preheat oven to 400°F (200°C).
2. Scramble the ground beef (or turkey) in a large skillet over medium heat until fully cooked. Drain excess fat if necessary.
3. Add the diced onions, celery, green beans, and carrots to the skillet. Cook for about three minutes.
4. Sprinkle the black pepper and granulated garlic over the mixture and stir well.
5. Continue cooking over medium-low heat until vegetables begin to soften, about 10 to 12 minutes.
6. Stir in the prepared gravy, ensuring it is thick enough. If too runny, add 1 tablespoon of flour, stir, and cook until mixture is bubbly.
7. Remove from heat and pour the meat and veggie mixture into a greased casserole dish.
8. Carefully spread the mashed potatoes over the top of the meat and vegetable mixture.
9. Sprinkle the dairy-free cheese blend evenly over the mashed potatoes.
10. Bake in the oven for about 16 minutes, or until the cheese is completely melted.
11. Allow to cool slightly before serving. Enjoy your allergen-free shepherd’s pie!
```

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Tree Nut-Free Meatball Subs**

**Ingredients:**

- 1 1/2 pounds ground sirloin
- 1 large egg, beaten
- 1 cup Italian bread crumbs (certified tree nut-free)
- 1 medium onion, chopped fine
- 4 cloves garlic, crushed and minced
- 1/2 teaspoon crushed red pepper flakes
- 2 teaspoons Worcestershire sauce (certified tree nut-free)
- 1/4 cup flat-leaf parsley leaves, chopped
- 1/4 cup grated Parmigiano or Romano (certified tree nut-free)
- Coarse salt and black pepper
- 2 tablespoons extra-virgin olive oil (certified tree nut-free)
- 4 cloves garlic, crushed and chopped
- 1/2 teaspoon crushed red pepper flakes
- 2 tablespoons flat-leaf parsley leaves, chopped
- 1/2 teaspoon dried oregano
- 1 (28 ounces) can crushed tomatoes (certified tree nut-free)
- 1 (14 ounces) can chunky style crushed tomatoes (certified tree nut-free)
- Salt and freshly ground black pepper
- 4 semolina crusty sub rolls (certified tree nut-free)
- 2 1/2 cups shredded provolone or Italian 4-cheese blend (certified tree nut-free)
- Shredded basil (sweet) or shredded arugula (spicy) leaves, for garnish

**Oven Fries (Accompaniment):**

- 4 medium white skinned potatoes, each cut into 8 wedges lengthwise
- Extra-virgin olive oil (certified tree nut-free), to coat
- Grill seasoning blend or coarse salt and black pepper

**Instructions:**

1. Preheat oven to 450 degrees F.
2. Place ground sirloin in a large mixing bowl and punch a well into the center of the meat.
3. Fill well with the egg, bread crumbs, onion, garlic, red pepper flakes, Worcestershire sauce, parsley, cheese, and a little salt and pepper.
4. Mix the meatball ingredients until well combined, yet not over-mixed.
5. Divide the mixture into 4 equal parts, roll each part into 4 balls and space equally onto a nonstick baking sheet.
6. Roast meatballs in the oven for about 12 minutes. Check a meatball to ensure it is cooked through before removing from the oven.
7. Heat a medium saucepan over medium heat. Add oil and garlic.
8. When garlic starts sizzling, add herbs and crushed red pepper. Allow oil to infuse for half a minute.
9. Stir in the tomatoes and season sauce with salt and pepper. Bring the sauce to a bubble, reduce heat, and simmer until meatballs are done.
10. Combine the meatballs and sauce and pile into sub rolls, 4 meatballs per sub.
11. Top with shredded cheese and place subs under the broiler to melt the cheese.
12. Top with shredded basil or arugula leaves and serve with oven fries.

**Oven Fries Instructions:**

1. Drizzle potatoes with a generous amount of extra-virgin olive oil.
2. Toss potatoes with grill seasoning blend or salt and pepper.
3. Place potatoes on a nonstick baking sheet and roast for 20 minutes or until just tender. Shake the baking sheet after 10 minutes to prevent sticking.
```

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

- There is a potential risk here since while the modified recipe states that all the specific ingredients are “certified tree nut-free,” the existence of this certification for ingredients can sometimes be ambiguous. Ensure that all manufacturers of the listed ingredients do indeed provide such certification to avoid cross-contamination risk.
- It's crucial to verify that the production and packaging facilities for these ingredients also maintain strict tree nut-free protocols to eliminate any chance of cross-contact.

```markdown
- 1 lb boneless chicken thighs, cubed
- 1 large onion, chopped
- 1/3 cup all-purpose flour
- 2 teaspoons Cajun seasoning (ensure it's shellfish-free)
- 1 3/4 cups water
- 1 1/2 cups corn
- 1 1/2 cups lima beans
- 2 medium carrots, sliced
- 1 (8 1/2 ounce) box cornbread mix (ensure it's shellfish-free)
- 1/3 cup milk
- 1 egg

**Directions:**
1. Preheat oven to 400 degrees F.

3. Add chicken and onion; sauté for 3-4 minutes until tender.
4. Sprinkle with Cajun seasoning and flour.

7. Bring to a boil.

9. Bring to a simmer.
10. Reduce heat to low.

13. Combine cornbread mix, milk, and egg; mix well.
14. Drop by spoonfuls over chicken mixture.
15. Spread gently to cover, leaving a 1/2-inch border.
16. Bake for 20 minutes or until cornbread is golden brown and filling is bubbly.
```

```markdown
#### Ingredients

- 9 ounces polenta instant yellow
- 2 tablespoons unsalted butter
- 2 teaspoons extra virgin olive oil
- 2 cups skim milk
- 2 tablespoons certified nut-free heavy cream
- 2 tablespoons rosemary leaves, chopped
- 1 tablespoon grated lemon peel, finely
- 1/4 cup grated nut-free certified Pecorino Romano cheese
- 2 teaspoons distilled white vinegar
- 8 eggs
- Arugula leaves to serve
- Nut-free certified tomato sauce to serve

#### Directions

1. Preheat the oven to 425°F. Lightly grease a foil-lined 11 x 7 inch baking pan.
2. Bring 4 cups of water to a boil. Gradually add the polenta, stirring vigorously. Stir in butter and olive oil. Reduce heat to medium. Cook for 2-3 minutes, stirring continuously. Stir in milk. Cook for another 2-3 minutes, stirring continuously. Add nut-free certified cream, rosemary, and lemon peel, stirring well. Pour the mixture evenly onto the prepared pan; smooth surface. Set aside to cool.
3. Cut the cooled polenta into fingers. Arrange the polenta fingers on a foil-lined baking sheet. Spray with no-stick cooking spray. Sprinkle with nut-free certified Pecorino Romano cheese.
4. Bake for 15-20 minutes until crisp and golden.
5. Meanwhile, bring 4 cups of water to a boil in a large saucepan. Stir in distilled white vinegar. Reduce heat to a gentle simmer. Break eggs into the water in batches of 1 or 2. Simmer for 2-3 minutes until whites are completely set and yolks begin to thicken. Remove with a slotted spoon.
6. Serve the poached eggs on a bed of arugula leaves and polenta fingers. Top with nut-free certified tomato sauce.
```

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

- Edibility and Nutritional Sense: The modified recipe maintains nutritional integrity and is edible, with substitutions that align closely with the original ingredients in terms of flavor and composition.

- Ingredient Safety: The modified recipe specifies that the heavy cream, Pecorino Romano cheese, and tomato sauce are certified nut-free, which addresses the potential cross-contamination risk associated with tree nut allergies. However, there is a need to ensure that all products and any new additions such as "extra virgin olive oil" also bear the certified nut-free label to ensure complete safety, as cross-contamination risk is crucial for allergies.

- Requirement Fulfillment: The requirement of being tree nut-free appears to be addressed by the certifications mentioned, but all ingredients should be meticulously checked to confirm their safety status, especially those not explicitly marked in the instructions.

- Cooking Steps: The steps are logical and feasible with the modified ingredients.

In summary, the recipe is cautiously likely to be valid if all nut-free certifications are thoroughly verified for each ingredient used, particularly non-certified oils or spices, to prevent any allergy risks.

Case 169-Title: Poppy Seed Bread
Ingredients: ["3 c. flour", "2 1/4 c. sugar", "1 1/8 c. oil", "1 1/2 c. milk", "3 eggs", "1 tsp. salt", "1 1/2 tsp. baking powder", "1 1/2 tsp. vanilla", "1 1/2 tsp. almond extract", "1 1/2 tsp. butter extract", "1 1/2 tsp. poppy seed"]
Directions: ["Mix all ingredients and bake in two greased loaf pans for 40 to 50 minutes at 350\u00b0.", "Poke holes in loaves with skewer when taken out of oven and while warm.", "Pour glaze over top."]
Requirement: Gluten-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Gluten-Free Poppy Seed Bread**

**Ingredients:**
- 2 1/2 c. gluten-free all-purpose flour blend (ensure it contains xanthan gum)
- 2 1/4 c. sugar
- 1 1/8 c. light olive oil
- 1 1/2 c. unsweetened almond milk (or other preferred plant-based milk)
- 3 large eggs
- 1 tsp. salt
- 1 1/2 tsp. gluten-free baking powder
- 1 1/2 tsp. pure vanilla extract
- 1 1/2 tsp. pure almond extract
- 1 1/2 tsp. butter-flavored extract (ensure gluten-free)
- 1 1/2 tsp. poppy seeds

**Directions:**
1. Preheat your oven to 350°F (175°C). Grease two loaf pans with a gluten-free non-stick spray or line them with parchment paper.
2. In a large mixing bowl, combine the gluten-free flour blend, sugar, salt, baking powder, and poppy seeds. Whisk together.
3. In another bowl, whisk together the olive oil, almond milk, eggs, vanilla extract, almond extract, and butter-flavored extract until well combined.
4. Pour the wet ingredients into the dry ingredients. Stir with a spatula or wooden spoon until just incorporated. Avoid overmixing.
5. Divide the batter evenly between the prepared loaf pans.
6. Bake in the preheated oven for 40 to 50 minutes, or until a toothpick inserted into the center comes out clean.
7. Remove loaves from the oven. While still warm, poke holes all over the top with a skewer.
8. Prepare your favorite gluten-free glaze, if desired, and pour over the warm loaves, allowing it to seep into the bread. Let the loaves cool completely before removing from the pans.
```

Case 170-Title: Banana Split Cake(Refrigerate)  
Ingredients: ["1 pkg. graham crackers, crushed", "2 sticks oleo", "2 1/2 c. powdered sugar", "2 egg whites", "4 bananas", "1 large can crushed pineapple", "1/2 c. maraschino cherries", "1/2 c. chopped pecans"]
Directions: ["Mix graham crackers, 1 stick oleo and 1/2 cup powdered sugar. Line bottom of a 9 x 13-inch baking dish; set aside."]
Requirement: Fish-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Modified Recipe: Banana Split Cake (Refrigerate, Fish-Free)**

**Ingredients:**
- 1 package graham crackers, crushed
- 1 stick unsalted butter (alternatively, dairy-free margarine), melted
- 2 1/2 cups powdered sugar
- 2 flax eggs (2 tablespoons ground flaxseed mixed with 6 tablespoons water, set aside to gel)
- 4 bananas, sliced
- 1 large can (20 oz) crushed pineapple, drained
- 1/2 cup maraschino cherries, rinsed and halved (ensure they're free from any additives that may contain allergens)
- 1/2 cup chopped pecans

**Directions:**
1. Mix the crushed graham crackers, melted unsalted butter, and 1/2 cup powdered sugar together until the mixture resembles wet sand.
2. Press this mixture firmly into the bottom of a 9 x 13-inch baking dish to create the crust. Set aside.
3. In a large bowl, combine the remaining 2 cups of powdered sugar with the prepared flax eggs, mixing until smooth.
4. Spread the flax egg mixture evenly over the graham cracker crust.
5. Layer the sliced bananas evenly over the flax mixture.
6. Evenly distribute the drained crushed pineapple over the banana layer.
7. Arrange the maraschino cherries evenly over the pineapple layer.
8. Sprinkle the chopped pecans over the top.
9. Cover and refrigerate the cake for at least 2 hours before serving to allow it to set.

Enjoy your fish-free, banana split cake!
```

Case 171-Title: St. Andre Walnut Cake
Ingredients: ["1 1/2 cups finely ground walnuts", "1/2 cup chopped walnuts", "4 eggs", "1 1/2 cups white sugar", "1 teaspoon vanilla extract", "1 teaspoon raspberry sauce", "1/2 cup all-purpose flour", "1 cup apricot preserves", "2 tablespoons brandy", "1 pint heavy whipping cream", "3/4 cup confectioners' sugar"]
Directions: ["Preheat oven to 350 degrees F (175 degrees C). Coat a 9 inch round cake pan with vegetable oil spray, and line the bottom with parchment paper.", "In a medium bowl, whip the eggs and sugar together until light. Stir in the vanilla and raspberry sauce. Toss the flour together with the walnuts, fold into the egg mixture. Pour into the prepared pan. Tap the pan firmly on the counter to remove air bubbles.", "Bake for 30 to 35 minutes in the preheated oven, until a toothpick inserted comes out clean. Cool cake in pan for 10 minutes before inverting onto a wire rack to cool completely. In a small saucepan, stir together the apricot preserves and brandy over medium heat until soft and liquidy. Strain and pour over cooled cake. Whip cream together with confectioners' sugar and vanilla until soft peaks form. Serve cake with a big dollop of whipped cream on the side."]
Requirement: Gluten-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Ingredients:**
- 1 1/2 cups finely ground walnuts
- 1/2 cup chopped walnuts
- 4 eggs
- 1 1/2 cups white sugar
- 1 teaspoon vanilla extract
- 1 teaspoon raspberry sauce
- 1/2 cup gluten-free all-purpose flour blend (ensure it contains xanthan gum or add 1/4 teaspoon xanthan gum separately)
- 1 cup apricot preserves (ensure gluten-free, without additives containing gluten)
- 2 tablespoons brandy
- 1 pint heavy whipping cream
- 3/4 cup confectioners' sugar (ensure gluten-free)

**Directions:**
1. Preheat oven to 350 degrees F (175 degrees C). Coat a 9-inch round cake pan with vegetable oil spray, and line the bottom with parchment paper.
2. In a medium bowl, whip the eggs and sugar together until light. Stir in the vanilla and raspberry sauce. Toss the gluten-free flour blend together with the walnuts, fold into the egg mixture. Pour into the prepared pan. Tap the pan firmly on the counter to remove air bubbles.
3. Bake for 30 to 35 minutes in the preheated oven, until a toothpick inserted comes out clean. Cool cake in pan for 10 minutes before inverting onto a wire rack to cool completely.
4. In a small saucepan, stir together the apricot preserves and brandy over medium heat until soft and liquidy. Strain and pour over cooled cake.
5. Whip cream together with confectioners' sugar and vanilla until soft peaks form. Serve cake with a big dollop of whipped cream on the side.
```
