Case 172-Title: 'rough Cut' Slow Cooker No-Beef Chili
Ingredients: ["2 tablespoons olive oil", "3 cups ham, cubed", "1 large onion, diced", "6 garlic cloves (roughly chopped)", "12 cup fresh parsley (roughly chopped)", "1 green serrano pepper", "2 red serrano peppers", "12 cup catsup", "15 ounces pinto beans (with juices)", "15 ounces small white beans (with juices)", "19 ounces black beans (with juices)", "28 ounces redpack diced tomatoes (Petite )", "14 12 ounces hunt's fire roasted diced tomatoes with garlic (optional)", "14 ounces chicken stock (optional) or 14 ounces beef stock (optional)", "1 cup red wine or 1 cup lager beer", "two teaspoons olive salad or two teaspoons sliced pimento olive", "i chili seasoning mix", "1 teaspoon black pepper", "2 teaspoons unsweetened cocoa powder", "4 -6 skinless chicken thighs", "chili powder"]
Directions: ["Turn on the cooker and set for four hours on HIGH.", "Add the ingredients in order ending with the chicken after adjusting the seasoning.", "Cook for 4hrs on high stirring once or twice or just leave it to simmer.", "Serve over rice or serve in large bowls with a warm toasty baguette.", "Some people will want even more beans so GO for it!", "As far as the cocoa powder is concerned -- I'm not going for a Mole Negro flavor.", "Just a depth of flavor."]

The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Modified Recipe: Rough Cut Slow Cooker No-Beef Chili**

**Ingredients:**
- 2 tablespoons olive oil
- 3 cups smoked tofu, cubed
- 1 large onion, diced
- 6 garlic cloves, roughly chopped
- 1/2 cup fresh parsley, roughly chopped
- 1 green serrano pepper, diced
- 2 red serrano peppers, diced
- 1/2 cup tomato sauce
- 15 ounces pinto beans, with juices
- 15 ounces small white beans, with juices
- 19 ounces black beans, with juices
- 28 ounces redpack diced tomatoes, petite
- 14 ounces hunt's fire-roasted diced tomatoes with garlic (optional)
- 14 ounces vegetable stock
- 1 cup non-alcoholic red wine or 1 cup non-alcoholic lager beer
- 2 teaspoons sliced pimento olives
- 1 chili seasoning mix (ensure mustard-free)
- 1 teaspoon black pepper
- 2 teaspoons unsweetened cocoa powder
- 1 tablespoon mild chili powder
- 4-6 ounces textured vegetable protein (TVP), rehydrated

**Instructions:**
1. Turn on the slow cooker and set it for four hours on HIGH.
2. In a skillet, heat the olive oil over medium heat. Add the cubed smoked tofu and cook until slightly browned. Transfer it to the slow cooker.
3. Add the onion, garlic, parsley, green and red serrano peppers to the slow cooker.
4. Stir in the tomato sauce, pinto beans, white beans, black beans, diced tomatoes, and fire-roasted tomatoes.
5. Pour in the vegetable stock and non-alcoholic red wine or lager beer.
6. Add the sliced pimento olives, chili seasoning mix, black pepper, cocoa powder, and chili powder to the slow cooker.
7. Add the rehydrated TVP to the mixture.
8. Adjust the spices if necessary, based on taste preference.
9. Cook for 4 hours on high, stirring once or twice, or leave it to simmer.
10. Serve the chili over rice or in large bowls with a warm toasty baguette if desired.
```

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

The modified recipe attempts to accommodate a mustard-free requirement, indicating that the chili seasoning mix should be mustard-free. However, it is crucial to ensure that all other components, such as any sauce, stock, or processed ingredients like tomato sauces and TVP, are also certified mustard-free as they could contain mustard-derived ingredients or have cross-contamination risks.

Make sure to check the labels or verify the mustard-free certification for these ingredients to fully comply with the requirement.

Now chop them up and place them in a bowl.", "Heat the olive oil in a large skillet over medium-high heat. Add the chopped tomatoes, along with any juices they've released since sitting in the bowl. Add 1/2 cup of water and allow to cook, uncovered, for 5 minutes, stirring occasionally.", "Remove the skillet from the heat and break the eggs into the tomatoes. Requirement: Wheat-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Modified Recipe: Skillet Eggs With Tomatoes, Parmigiano-Reggiano & Basil (Wheat-Free)**

**Ingredients:**
- 1 1/2 tablespoons extra virgin olive oil
- 8 eggs, extra large
- 1 3/4 pounds fresh Roma tomatoes, chopped (about 6)
- 1 handful fresh basil leaves
- 1 cup freshly-grated Parmigiano-Reggiano
- Sea salt and fresh-cracked black pepper to taste

**Instructions:**
1. Optional step: Remove the skin off the tomatoes. Bring a medium-sized pot of water to a boil and add the tomatoes, allowing them to cook for 1 minute. Immediately remove them. Once they've cooled, remove their skins with your hands. Slice them in half, remove the seeds and the hard section that connected them to the vine. Chop them up and place them in a bowl.
   
2. Heat the extra virgin olive oil in a large skillet over medium-high heat. Add the chopped tomatoes, along with any juices they've released while sitting in the bowl. You should hear a sizzle when they hit the pan. Add a little sea salt and stir. Add 1/2 cup of water and cook, uncovered, for 5 minutes, stirring occasionally.
   
3. Remove the skillet from the heat and break the eggs into the tomatoes. Keep them in couples when you break them, as it becomes easier to portion out later. Add sea salt and a good crack of black pepper to each egg and return to the heat. Lower the flame to medium. Sprinkle the Parmigiano-Reggiano over the eggs and tomatoes, ensuring all eggs are covered. Cover and cook for 3 to 5 minutes, depending on your preferred yolk consistency.
   
4. Add the basil leaves as soon as you remove the skillet from the heat. Serve immediately, optionally with a side of gluten-free bread.
```

**Directions:**

Case 179-Title: Strawberry Rice
Ingredients: ["1 (3 oz.) pkg. strawberry jello", "2 c. cooked white rice", "1/4 c. sugar", "1/2 tsp. vanilla", "1 c. strawberries, sliced or 10 oz. frozen strawberries, drained and thawed", "1/2 pt. whipping cream", "1/4 c. powdered sugar"]
Directions: ["Mix jello according to directions on package.", "When set, add rice, granulated sugar and vanilla.", "Mix well until blended.", "Fold in strawberries.", "Whip cream with powdered sugar until stiff. Fold into gelatin mixture.", "Chill several hours or overnight. Serves 10 to 12."]
Requirement: Tree nut-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Strawberry Rice (Tree Nut-Free)**

**Ingredients:**
- 1 (3 oz.) pkg. strawberry gelatin (ensure it's tree nut-free)
- 2 cups cooked white rice
- 1/4 cup granulated sugar
- 1/2 teaspoon vanilla extract
- 1 cup fresh strawberries, sliced or 10 oz. frozen strawberries, drained and thawed
- 1/2 pint heavy whipping cream
- 1/4 cup confectioners' sugar

**Directions:**
1. Prepare the strawberry gelatin according to the package instructions. Allow it to set in the refrigerator.
2. Once the gelatin is set, add the cooked rice, granulated sugar, and vanilla extract to the gelatin. Mix well until blended.
3. Gently fold in the sliced or thawed strawberries.
4. In a separate bowl, whip the heavy cream with the confectioners' sugar until stiff peaks form.
5. Carefully fold the whipped cream into the gelatin mixture until well combined.
6. Chill the mixture in the refrigerator for several hours or overnight before serving.
```

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

While the modification indicates an attempt to ensure the strawberry gelatin is tree nut-free, it is crucial to verify that all ingredients, especially processed ones, are explicitly certified as tree nut-free. Case 181-Title: Acorn Squash Stuffed With Carrot, Apple And Onion Couscous Recipe
Ingredients: ["1/3 c. Toasted Israeli Style couscous", "2 c. water", "1/2 x tomato bouillon cube", "1 x acorn squash", "1 x celery stalk", "1 x carrot", "1/2 sm onion", "1/2 x apple cored", "2 Tbsp. Romano cheese", "1 Tbsp. finely minced fresh basil salt and black pepper", "2 tsp unsalted butter"]
Directions: ["Make couscous in water seasoned with tomato bouillon.", "Drain, Reserving liquid.", "Cut a hole in the acorn squash to act as a vent.", "Microwave on high for 6 min.", "Let stand.", "When cold sufficient to touch, halve lengthwise.", "Remove seeds.", "In bowl of food processor, coarsely chop onion, celery, carrot and apple.", "In a large mixing bowl combine the minced vegetables and apple with the liquid removed couscous.", "Season with cheese, basil and a generous healthy pinch of salt and pepper.", "Add in sufficient of the reserved liquid to moisten the mix.", "Reserving 1 c. of the stuffing, place the stuffing mix in an oven proof casserole.", "Add in the rest of the broth reserved from the couscous.", "Place each squash half in the casserole, cavity side up.", "Sprinkle lightly with salt and pepper.", "Fill each squash with the remaining stuffing.", "Add in a pad of butter on each.", "Cover loosely with foil.", "Bake in a preheat 400F oven for 25 to 35 min.", "Serve warm.", "Untested variation (suggested by techniques used in original recipe): don't precook the squash or possibly the couscous.", "Mix the raw vegetables, crumbled bouillon and couscous.", "Stuff raw squash.", "Steam for 20 to 30 min till done.", "Brown under the broiler (optional).", "NOTES :This recipe has been on my \"to try\" list since Nanette posted it on the VegRecipes list on 08 Feb 2001.", "I thought it would make a full meal when mixed with large Couscous - a variation on the original recipe.", "We use one-third box of Osem's Mediterranean Couscous and 1/3 of the enclosed tomato basil bouillon cube.", "This is comfort food."]
Requirement: Celery-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Modified Recipe for Acorn Squash Stuffed With Carrot, Apple And Onion Couscous**

Ingredients:
- 1/3 cup Toasted Israeli Style couscous
- 2 cups water
- 1/2 small tomato bouillon cube
- 1 acorn squash
- 1 medium zucchini (as a substitute for celery)
- 1 carrot
- 1/2 small onion
- 1/2 apple cored
- 2 tablespoons Romano cheese
- 1 tablespoon finely minced fresh basil
- Salt and black pepper to taste
- 2 teaspoons unsalted butter

Directions:
1. Make couscous in water seasoned with tomato bouillon. Drain, reserving liquid.
2. Cut a hole in the acorn squash to act as a vent. Microwave on high for 6 minutes. Let stand.
3. When cool enough to touch, halve lengthwise and remove seeds.
4. In bowl of food processor, coarsely chop onion, zucchini, carrot, and apple.
5. In a large mixing bowl, combine the minced vegetables and apple with the liquid-drained couscous.
6. Season with cheese, basil, and a generous pinch of salt and pepper.
7. Add sufficient reserved liquid to moisten the mixture.
8. Reserving 1 cup of the stuffing, place the remaining stuffing mixture in an ovenproof casserole.
9. Add the rest of the broth reserved from the couscous.
10. Place each squash half in the casserole, cavity side up. Sprinkle lightly with salt and pepper.
11. Fill each squash with the remaining stuffing.
12. Add a pad of butter on each.
13. Cover loosely with foil. Bake in a preheated 400°F oven for 25 to 35 minutes.
14. Serve warm.
```

- 1 cup chopped green onions

Bring the mixture to a boil; reduce the heat to medium and boil for 5 minutes.", "Remove from the heat and stir in the vanilla.", "Beat for 3 minutes until thickens and stir in the peanuts.", "Drop by tablespoon full onto wax paper and allow candy to harden.", "Store in an airtight container.", "For gifts, give in tins."]
Requirement: Tree nut-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Dish Name:** Tree Nut-Free Peanut Patties

**Ingredients:**
- 1 1/2 cups sugar
- 1 (3 ounce) package corn starch-based vanilla pudding mix (not instant, ensure tree nut-free label)
- 3/4 cup evaporated milk
- 1 teaspoon vanilla extract
- 2 cups roasted sunflower seeds (ensure tree nut-free label)

**Directions:**
1. Combine the sugar, pudding mix, and milk in a medium saucepan over medium-high heat, stirring frequently. Bring the mixture to a boil; reduce the heat to medium and boil for 5 minutes.
2. Remove from heat and stir in the vanilla extract.
3. Beat the mixture for 3 minutes until it thickens, then stir in the roasted sunflower seeds.
4. Drop by tablespoonful onto wax paper and allow the candy to harden.
5. Store in an airtight container. For gifts, give in tins.
```

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

Case 185-Title: French Silk Chocolate Pie Ii
Ingredients: ["1 cup butter", "1 1/2 cups white sugar", "4 tablespoons unsweetened cocoa powder", "2 teaspoons vanilla extract", "4 eggs", "1 (9 inch) pie crust, baked"]
Directions: ["Cream butter and sugar. Blend in cocoa and vanilla. Beating at high speed, add one egg and beat until thoroughly incorporated. Repeat with each remaining egg. Keep whipping until fluffy. Spread in cooked pie shell of choice and keep refrigerated"]
Requirement: Sulfite-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Modified Recipe: French Silk Chocolate Pie II (Sulfite-Free)**

**Ingredients:**
- 1 cup sulfite-free unsalted butter
- 1 1/2 cups organic cane sugar (ensure sulfite-free)
- 4 tablespoons unsweetened cocoa powder
- 2 teaspoons organic pure vanilla extract (certified sulfite-free)
- 4 large eggs (preferably organic and certified sulfite-free)
- 1 homemade 9-inch pie crust (recipe below ensures sulfite-free)

**Homemade Sulfite-Free Pie Crust:**
- 1 1/4 cups all-purpose flour (check to ensure sulfite-free)
- 1/2 cup sulfite-free cold unsalted butter, diced
- 1/4 teaspoon sea salt
- 3-4 tablespoons ice water

**Directions:**

1. **Prepare the Homemade Pie Crust:**
   - In a large bowl, mix the flour and sea salt together. Add the diced butter.
   - Using a pastry cutter or your fingers, work the butter into the flour mixture until it resembles coarse crumbs.
   - Add ice water, one tablespoon at a time, mixing until the dough sticks together without being sticky.
   - Form the dough into a disk, wrap in plastic wrap, and refrigerate for at least 30 minutes.
   - Preheat the oven to 375°F (190°C). Roll out the dough on a floured surface and fit it into a 9-inch pie plate.
   - Trim excess dough, leaving about an inch overhang, then fold under and crimp edges. Prick the bottom with a fork.
   - Line with parchment paper, fill with pie weights or dried beans, and bake for 15 minutes.
   - Remove weights and parchment, then bake for another 10-12 minutes until golden. Cool completely.

2. **Make the Filling:**
   - In a large mixing bowl, cream the sulfite-free butter and cane sugar until light and fluffy.
   - Mix in the unsweetened cocoa powder and certified sulfite-free vanilla extract.
   - On high speed, add one egg at a time, beating thoroughly after each addition until the mixture is light and fluffy.

3. **Assemble the Pie:**
   - Spread the chocolate filling evenly into the prepared sulfite-free pie crust.
   - Refrigerate for at least 2 hours before serving to allow the filling to set.

**Enjoy this sulfite-free French Silk Chocolate Pie with assurance of safety and a rich chocolate flavor!**
```

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

The modified recipe effectively makes adjustments to cater to a sulfite-free requirement by selecting ingredients labeled as sulfite-free. However, some potential risks need attention:

1. **Ingredient Safety and Cross-Contamination:**
   - Ensure that all ingredients used, such as flour, butter, sugar, and vanilla extract, are not only labeled sulfite-free but also tested for potential cross-contamination during manufacturing. It is crucial to verify certifications or contact manufacturers if necessary.
   
2. **Egg Certification:**
   - While eggs inherently do not contain sulfites, the modification suggests obtaining certified sulfite-free eggs. Ensure such certification or consult your supplier for assurance as "sulfite-free" labeling on eggs is uncommon due to natural absence.

3. **General Ingredient Handling:**
   - Maintain dedicated kitchen tools and storage areas to avoid cross-contamination with sulfite-containing products. This is especially important in shared kitchens.

If these potential risks are managed carefully, the modified recipe should meet the requirement for a sulfite-free diet.

```markdown
### Modified Tortilla Soup with Lentils

#### Ingredients:
- 1/4 cup sesame-free extra-virgin olive oil (check label for certification)
- 1 medium onion, finely chopped
- 2 bell peppers, finely chopped
- 1 jalapeno, seeded and chopped
- 1 clove garlic, minced
- 1 tablespoon chili powder
- 1 teaspoon cumin
- 1 teaspoon unsweetened cocoa powder
- 1/2 teaspoon Mexican oregano
- 1/2 teaspoon paprika
- 1/2 teaspoon cayenne pepper
- Pinch of crushed red pepper
- 1/2 teaspoon kosher salt, plus more to taste
- Fresh ground black pepper, to taste
- 1 pound sesame-free ground chicken or turkey
- One 28-ounce can diced tomatoes
- 4 cups sesame-free vegetable stock (ensure it's certified sesame-free)
- 1 cup lentils, rinsed
- Sesame-free oil, for frying tortilla strips (ensure certification)
- Six 4-inch corn tortillas, cut into 1/2-inch strips
- 2 lime wedges, plus 4-6 more for serving

#### Directions:
1. Heat the sesame-free olive oil in a large pot over moderately high heat.
2. Add the onion and bell peppers and cook, stirring occasionally, until the onions are soft and translucent, about 5 to 7 minutes.
3. Add the jalapeno and garlic, cooking for an additional minute until fragrant.
4. Add the chili powder, cumin, cocoa, oregano, paprika, cayenne, crushed red pepper, 1/2 teaspoon of salt, and a few grinds of black pepper. Add the ground chicken or turkey, and cook, breaking it up with a wooden spoon, until browned and cooked through, about 7 minutes.
5. Stir in the diced tomatoes and the certified sesame-free vegetable stock. Bring the mixture to a boil.
6. Stir in the lentils, reduce the heat to a simmer, and cook until the lentils are tender, about 30 to 35 minutes.
7. Meanwhile, heat 1/2 inch of sesame-free oil in a skillet over moderate heat until shimmering.
8. Fry the tortilla strips in batches for 3 minutes or until crispy.
9. Transfer the fried tortilla strips to a paper towel-lined plate, sprinkle with salt, and squeeze with lime while still hot.
10. Ladle the soup into bowls and serve with tortilla strips, lime wedges, diced avocado, dairy-free and sesame-free sour cream, fresh cilantro, and dairy-free sesame-free cheese alternatives.
```

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

The modified recipe aims to address a sesame-free requirement by substituting all potentially sesame-containing ingredients with their sesame-free alternatives. However, several points need to be closely monitored:

1. **Ingredient Certification**: It is necessary that all ingredients substituted for sesame-free versions, such as olive oil, vegetable stock, oil for frying, dairy-free sour cream, and cheese alternatives, have explicit sesame-free certification. Lack of such certification might still pose a risk of cross-contamination.

2. **Cross-contamination and Cross-reactivity Risk**: Ensure that the kitchen and cooking tools used are thoroughly cleaned to prevent cross-contact with sesame. Ensure sesame is not used in preparing other dishes in the same vicinity to avoid airborne sesame particles.

By closely managing these points, the modified recipe can potentially be sesame-free. However, without explicit certifications and stringent handling practices, there remains a risk of unintentional sesame exposure.

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Dish Name:** Korean Bulgogi Tacos (Egg-Free)

**Ingredients:**
- 1 pound Marinated Flank Steak (see below recipe)
- 1/2 cup "Korean Red Dragon" Sauce (ensure egg-free, or see recipe box)
- 1/2 whole English Cucumber, Sliced for Pickling (see below)
- 1/2 whole Red Onion, Chopped
- 1/2 cup Store-bought Organic Kimchi (ensure egg-free)
- 1/4 cup Chopped Cilantro
- 1 whole Mexican Red Chile or Jalapeno, Trimmed, Seeded, Minced
- 3 whole Limes, Cut in Half and Then Into Quarters
- 10 whole Flour or Corn Tortillas (ensure egg-free)
- 1 pound Flank Steak
- 1/4 cup Tamari or Soy Sauce (ensure egg-free)
- 1/4 cup Brown Sugar
- 2 Tablespoons Sake
- 1 Tablespoon Toasted Sesame Oil
- 3 whole Cloves Garlic, Thinly Sliced
- 2 stalks Scallions, Both White and Green Parts, Trimmed and Minced
- 1 Tablespoon Roasted Sesame Seeds
- 1/4 teaspoon Ground Black Pepper
- 1/2 whole English Cucumber, Sliced
- 1 Tablespoon Sugar
- 1 teaspoon Kosher Salt, or More to Taste

**Directions for Bulgogi:**
1. Combine soy sauce, brown sugar, sake, sesame oil, garlic, scallions, sesame seeds, and black pepper in a bowl. Whisk until the sugar dissolves.
2. Pour the marinade over the flank steak in a zip-lock bag; toss thoroughly to coat.
3. Marinate in the fridge for at least 3 hours or overnight, turning the bag once.
4. When ready to grill, preheat to high.
5. Grill the steak for about 7 minutes on each side or to your desired level of doneness, turning once with tongs.
6. When done, let it sit for 5 minutes before cutting it.
7. Cut diagonally, against the grain into strips, and cut strips into bite-sized pieces.

**Directions for Pickled Cucumber:**
1. Place cucumber slices in a bowl, add salt and sugar.
2. Use hands to mix and coat them evenly.
3. Let sit in the fridge for at least 15 minutes for flavor to develop.

**To Assemble Tacos:**
1. Grill tortillas for 30 seconds on each side and wrap them in a towel to keep warm; set aside.
2. On a tortilla, add meat in preferred amount.
3. Pour 1 teaspoon of Korean Dragon Sauce over the meat.
4. Add red onions, kimchi (a few pieces), cucumber (3 slices or more), red chile, cilantro, and lime (optional).
5. Wrap and enjoy!
```

**Dish Name:** Vegan Made-In-The-Pan Chocolate Cake

- 1 teaspoon vanilla extract

8. Pour 1 teaspoon of vinegar into a small dent.

10. Start stirring (slowly) with A FORK.

12. Smooth out the cake.
13. Put into the oven for 30 minutes.

**Dish Name:** Wheat-Free Chicken Casserole

**Ingredients:**
- 6 lb. chicken
- 1 large onion
- 1 can (10.5 oz) gluten-free mushroom soup
- 1 can (10.5 oz) gluten-free cream of chicken soup
- 1 pint lactose-free sour cream
- 3 cups gluten-free cornmeal stuffing mix
- Salt and pepper to taste
- 2 tbsp olive oil

**Directions:**
1. Reserve chicken broth by boiling the chicken with the onion in water until fully cooked. Remove the chicken, set aside to cool, and keep the broth.
2. Cut the cooled chicken into bite-size pieces.

5. In a greased baking dish, spread the chicken mixture evenly. Top with the moistened stuffing mix.
6. Preheat the oven to 350°F (175°C). Bake the casserole for approximately 45 minutes to 1 hour, or until the top is golden and the casserole is heated through.

```

```markdown
**Dish Name:** English Peas Cheese Tartlets (Mustard-Free)

**Modified Recipe:**
Ingredients:
- 1/2 cup coconut milk (full-fat)
- 3 cloves garlic, finely chopped
- 3 shallots, finely chopped
- 8-ounce package frozen peas, thawed
- 1/2 cup grated Parmesan (certified mustard-free)
- 1/8 teaspoon ground nutmeg
- Salt and freshly ground black pepper
- 16 (2-inch) gluten-free tartlet shells (certified mustard-free)

**Instructions:**
1. In a saucepan over low heat, combine the coconut milk, garlic, and shallots. Simmer and reduce by about 1/3.
2. Preheat the oven to 300 degrees F.
3. Add peas, half of the certified mustard-free Parmesan, nutmeg, and salt and pepper to the coconut milk mixture. Continue to reduce until it reaches a medium thickness, then let cool.
4. Place a spoonful of the pea mixture into each tartlet shell.
5. Sprinkle the reserved Parmesan on top of each tartlet.
6. Brown in the oven for a few minutes until the tops are golden, and serve hot.

Case 195-Title: Argentinean Beef Saute
Ingredients: ["1 lb. ground round", "3 medium onions, chopped", "1 large green pepper, chopped", "1 tsp. basil", "1/2 tsp. pepper", "1/4 tsp. oregano", "1/4 tsp. sugar", "3 cloves garlic", "2 Tbsp. parsley, chopped", "1 (8 oz.) can red kidney beans, reserve liquid", "1 (8 oz.) can hominy, drained"]
Directions: ["In large heavy skillet over medium heat, brown beef. Add onions and green pepper. Saute until vegetables are tender.", "Stir in rest of ingredients.", "Simmer, uncovered, gradually adding 1/4 cup bean liquid.", "Stir occasionally about 10 minutes or until flavors blend.", "Serves 4."]
Requirement: Mustard-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Dish Name:** Modified Argentinean Beef Saute (Mustard-free)

**Ingredients:**
- 1 lb. ground beef (round)
- 3 medium onions, chopped
- 1 large green pepper, chopped
- 1 tsp. dried basil
- 1/2 tsp. black pepper
- 1/4 tsp. dried oregano
- 1/4 tsp. sugar
- 3 cloves garlic, minced
- 2 Tbsp. fresh parsley, chopped
- 1 (8 oz.) can red kidney beans, reserve liquid
- 1 (8 oz.) can hominy, drained

**Directions:**
1. In a large heavy skillet over medium heat, brown the ground beef, breaking it into crumbles as it cooks.
2. Add the chopped onions and green pepper to the beef. Sauté the mixture until the vegetables become tender.
3. Stir in the dried basil, black pepper, dried oregano, sugar, and minced garlic.
4. Add the chopped parsley, red kidney beans, and hominy to the skillet, stirring to combine all ingredients.
5. Gradually add 1/4 cup of the reserved bean liquid to the skillet, mixing thoroughly.
6. Allow the mixture to simmer, uncovered, for about 10 minutes or until the flavors blend together, stirring occasionally.
7. Once done, serve the Argentinean Beef Sauté warm. Serves 4.
```

Case 196-Title: Souffléd Macaroni And Cheese
Ingredients: ["1 1/2 cups scalded whole milk", "1 cup fresh bread crumbs plus more for the top", "2 cups grated cheese, I used cheddar, gruyere and St Andre use what you like and grate a little more cheddar and gruyere for the top", "1 cup cooked macaroni", "3 large eggs separated", "1/4 cup diced pimento's", "1 tablespoon chopped parsley", "1 teaspoon salt", "3 tablespoons melted butter"]
Directions: ["Pre heat oven to 375 degree's", "Pour milk over bread crumbs, add cheese. Cover and let stand until cheese melts. Add macaroni. Combine and add beaten egg yolks, pimento, parsley, onion, salt and buttter. Beat the egg whites until stiff but not dry and fold into the mixture. Note: I sprinkled the top of the mac and cheese with breadcrumbs and grated some cheddar and gruyere on top.", "Bake for approximately 30-35 minutes until cheese is melted and top is browned."]
Requirement: Soy-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Dish Name:** Souffléd Macaroni And Cheese (Soy-Free Version)

**Ingredients:**
- 1 1/2 cups scalded whole milk
- 1 cup fresh bread crumbs plus more for the top (Ensure the bread is soy-free)
- 2 cups grated cheese (e.g., cheddar, gruyere; ensure no soy additives)
- 1 cup cooked macaroni (check for soy-free pasta)
- 3 large eggs, separated
- 1/4 cup diced pimentos (check for soy-free packaging)
- 1 tablespoon chopped parsley
- 1 teaspoon salt
- 3 tablespoons unsalted butter (verify no soy additives)

**Directions:**
1. Preheat oven to 375 degrees Fahrenheit.
2. Pour the scalded milk over the bread crumbs in a large mixing bowl. Add the grated cheese. Cover and let the mixture stand until the cheese melts.
3. Add the cooked macaroni to the cheese mixture and stir to combine.
4. In a separate bowl, beat the egg yolks. Add the beaten yolks, diced pimentos, chopped parsley, salt, and melted butter to the macaroni and cheese mixture. Mix well.
5. In another clean, dry bowl, beat the egg whites until stiff but not dry. Gently fold the beaten egg whites into the macaroni mixture until well combined.
6. Transfer the mixture to a baking dish. Sprinkle additional bread crumbs and grated cheese on top for a crispy crust.
7. Bake in the preheated oven for approximately 30-35 minutes, or until the cheese is melted and the top is browned.
```

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

2. Requirement Fulfillment: Check for hidden soy derivatives or additives in the cheese, pimentos, and butter, as these can often contain soy lecithin or other soy-based components. It's also essential that all packaging and processing equipment are verified to be free from cross-contamination with soy.

```markdown
**Modified Recipe: The Best Ribs U Ever Ate (Celery-Free)**

**Ingredients:**
- Enough ribs (get about 1 1/2 lb. per person)
- 1 container of a celery-free barbecue sauce (e.g., Annie's Organic Original BBQ Sauce)
- 1 teaspoon garlic powder
- 2 tablespoons coconut sugar

**Directions:**
1. Preheat the oven to 350°F.
2. Fill a broiler pan with about 1/2 inch of water.
3. Lay out the ribs on the broiler and sprinkle with garlic powder.
4. Cover the ribs with aluminum foil, sealing around the edges so that the steam helps to cook the meat.
5. Cook for 1 1/2 hours at 350°F in the oven. Then take out of oven, remove the foil, and turn the ribs over.
6. Sprinkle with garlic powder, check the water level in the bottom of the broiler, re-cover with foil, and cook for another 1 1/2 hours at 350°F.
```

Case 199-Title: Bacon Cheese Stuffed Shells
Ingredients: ["24 uncooked jumbo pasta shells", "1 cup chopped fresh mushrooms", "1 cup finely chopped onion", "1 tablespoon butter, divided", "1/4 cup butter, divided", "1 1/2 cups ricotta cheese", "1 (8 ounce) package cream cheese, softened, divided", "1 1/2 cups asiago cheese, divided", "1 cup shredded parmesan cheese", "1 cup crumbled cooked bacon", "2 tablespoons minced fresh parsley, divided", "1/2 teaspoon garlic salt", "1/2 teaspoon ground nutmeg", "1/4 teaspoon pepper", "2 tablespoons flour", "2 cups heavy whipping cream", "1/2 cup chicken broth", "1/2 cup 2% milk", "2 cups shredded romano cheese", "1 1/2 cups shredded mozzarella cheese"]
Directions: ["Cook pasta. Meanwhile in a large skillet saute mushrooms and onions in 1 T butter until tender.", "In a large bowl beat ricotta and 1/2 cream cheese until blended. Stir 1/2 c Asiago cheese, Parmesan cheese, bacon, 1 T parsley, garlic salt, nutmeg, pepper and mushroom mixture. Spoon into shells, place in a greased 9x13 baking dish.", "In a large saucepan melt remaining butter. Stir in flour until smooth, gradually adding the cream, broth and milk. Bring to a boil, cook and stir for 1-2 minutes or until thickened.", "Stir in Romano cheese and the remaining cream cheese, Asiago and parsley. Pour over shells. Sprinkle with mozzarella cheese. Cover and bake at 350 for 30 minutes. Uncover and bake 10-15 minutes longer or until bubbly."]
Requirement: Peanut-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Dish Name:** Bacon Cheese Stuffed Shells (Peanut-Free)

**Ingredients:**

- 24 uncooked jumbo pasta shells
- 1 cup chopped fresh mushrooms
- 1 cup finely chopped onion
- 3 tablespoons unsalted butter, divided
- 1 1/2 cups ricotta cheese
- 4 ounces cream cheese, softened
- 1 1/2 cups asiago cheese, divided
- 1 cup shredded parmesan cheese
- 1 cup cooked and crumbled bacon (ensure bacon is certified peanut-free)
- 2 tablespoons minced fresh parsley, divided
- 1/2 teaspoon garlic salt
- 1/2 teaspoon ground nutmeg
- 1/4 teaspoon pepper
- 2 tablespoons all-purpose flour
- 2 cups heavy whipping cream
- 1/2 cup low-sodium chicken broth
- 1/2 cup 2% milk
- 2 cups shredded romano cheese
- 1 1/2 cups shredded mozzarella cheese

**Instructions:**

1. Cook pasta shells according to package directions; drain and set aside.
2. In a large skillet, melt 1 tablespoon of the butter over medium heat. Add mushrooms and onions; sauté until tender.
3. In a large bowl, beat together ricotta and 4 ounces cream cheese until well mixed. Stir in 1/2 cup asiago cheese, parmesan cheese, crumbled bacon, 1 tablespoon minced parsley, garlic salt, nutmeg, pepper, and the mushroom mixture.
4. Spoon the cheese mixture into each shell and place the filled shells in a greased 9x13-inch baking dish.
5. In a large saucepan, melt the remaining 2 tablespoons of butter over medium heat. Stir in flour until smooth and gradually whisk in the cream, chicken broth, and milk. Bring to a gentle boil, stirring constantly, and cook until thickened, about 1-2 minutes.
6. Stir in romano cheese, the remaining asiago cheese, remaining cream cheese, and remaining parsley until melted and well combined.
7. Pour the sauce evenly over the stuffed shells in the baking dish. Sprinkle with mozzarella cheese.
8. Cover with foil and bake in a preheated 350°F oven for 30 minutes. Uncover and bake an additional 10-15 minutes, or until bubbly and golden on top.
```

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution 

The modified recipe claims to be peanut-free, but the verification of peanut-free certification is mentioned only for the bacon. While this provides some confidence regarding the bacon, additional ingredients such as butter, cheese, and other dairy components, as well as the pasta shells, could potentially be exposed to cross-contamination during manufacturing unless explicitly stated in the ingredient sourcing. It's crucial to ensure that all ingredients are certified peanut-free or sourced from trusted suppliers free from cross-contamination. 

Check all ingredient packaging labels or suppliers' assurances for explicit confirmation of a peanut-free status to avoid potential risks before proceeding with the recipe.
